Chengdu Special Correspondence

Reorganization of the Sichuan Army 33

The Sichuan Provincial Governor's Office convened a military affairs conference for the 25th year [of the Republic] on September 24th at 9:00 AM, officially opening at the joint office of the provincial government. The conference was scheduled for two days, with a break on the 25th and continuing on the 26th, which was the last day of the conference. Because the attendees were all important generals directly under the jurisdiction of the Sichuan Rehabilitation Supervising Office, the Duyuan Street, where the provincial government was located, was heavily guarded on the 24th. Attendees included Liu Xiang, the Rehabilitation Supervisor; Tang Shizun, Commander of the 21st Army; Pan Wenhua, Commander of the 23rd Army; Wang Lingxu, Commander of the 44th Army; Division Commanders Fan Shaozeng, Yang Guozhen, Rao Guohua, Chen Lanting, Chen Qian, Xu Yaoqing, and Guo Zhuqi; as well as affiliated brigade commanders, Chief of Staff of the Supervisor's Office Chuan Chang, Adjutant General Liang Jun, Chief of the Staff Office Yan Xiaohu, Chief of the Military Affairs Office Xu Enping, Chief of the Secretariat Liu Dongfu, Chief of the Military Affairs Office Min Yonglian, Chief of the Military Medical Office Zhao Bojun, Chief of the Management Office Tang Hua, and Secretary-General of the Provincial Government Deng Mingjie, totaling more than 200 people. It was the largest gathering in the past two years. The topics of discussion included military supplies, military strength, military affairs, training, and the allocation of troop stations. During the meeting on the 26th, Supervisor Liu also invited Yan Yangchu, Deputy Chairman of the Provincial Government Design Committee, to give a lecture. The contents of this conference were kept strictly confidential, and all levels of participants were strictly ordered by the Supervisor's Office not to disclose any information. The importance of its nature can be imagined, and it is undoubtedly related to the future of Sichuan. Therefore, I will summarize the situation from various sources, as follows.

End of Bandit Suppression Campaign

The military affairs of bandit suppression in Sichuan Province came to a conclusion after Chairman Chiang Kai-shek entered Sichuan in the last quarter of the 24th year and ordered the armies to launch a large-scale campaign. At that time, the bandits, with their remaining forces, took the route from Songpan and Maogong in western Sichuan and fled into Xikang, plotting to occupy a corner, restore their strength, and then plan to invade again. Later, the two groups of Zhu De and Mao Zedong, and Xiao Ke and He Long, successively entered Kang and joined forces with the Xu Xiangqian bandits. From then on, the Xikang region became the focus of bandit suppression. The Central Army and the Sichuan and Yunnan garrison forces successively entered Kang, encircling them heavily. Although the bandit forces joined forces, they suffered great losses due to years of resistance, and the Zhu De, Mao Zedong, and Xiao Ke, He Long bandits had been fleeing for several provinces and were exhausted. How could they resist such a large number of government troops? Therefore, they changed their plan, abandoned Xikang, and joined forces with the Xu Xiangqian bandits in northern Shaanxi, attempting to flee into Suining and open up the so-called international route. In July and August of this year, the bandits fled from northern Kang, passing through the Sichuan-Qinghai border and entering Gansu. At that time, the situation in Songpan, Maogong and other places in western Sichuan seemed very tense. However, the armies in Sichuan had long been strictly prepared, so the bandit forces were severely attacked upon arrival and fled into southern Gansu. At this point, the military affairs of bandit suppression in Sichuan came to an end. However, the bandit forces were constantly fleeing, and the Central Government, in addition to increasing the deployment of Hu Zongnan's entire army to Gansu to cooperate with the units of Zhu Shaoliang, Yu Xuezhong, etc., to intensify the suppression in order to annihilate them in one fell swoop, also transferred the main forces of Sun Zhen's 41st Army and Deng Xihou's 45th Army from Sichuan Province. On the 23rd and 24th, the two units had set out separately. Dong and Zeng's divisions of the 41st Army were stationed in Bikou and Chengdu, Gansu, to carry out suppression as the opportunity arose, while Chen's division of the 45th Army was stationed in Guangyuan, Yangpingguan, and Lueyang in Shaanxi to prevent the bandits from fleeing.

Four Major Issues Currently

Now that the military affairs of bandit suppression have come to an end, the future problems in Sichuan Province are: (1) the reorganization of the army, (2) the allocation of stations, (3) local rehabilitation, and (4) military expenses. Among them, the last one is the most urgent to solve at present. It is necessary to say that the military expenses of Sichuan Province have been reviewed and approved at more than 60 million per year, and have been decreasing year by year since the 25th year [of the Republic]. It is difficult to have a fixed mechanism for appropriation, but due to temporary difficulties in raising funds, the military salaries of various armies have been in arrears for several months. Any undertaking takes economics as a prerequisite, and the army is no exception. Without solving the problem of military expenses, how can we talk about engaging in reorganization? Therefore, the purpose of this military affairs conference convened by the Supervisor's Office is to seek a proper solution so that the aforementioned arrears of salaries can be gradually paid off, and so that it will not be difficult to raise funds in the future. Then, the distribution of other stations and the reorganization problems will not be difficult to solve. Regarding local rehabilitation, the first priority is to eliminate bandits, and the second is to revitalize the government. Since the defeat of the bandit army, the authorities have been determined to govern, and progress has been made in recent years. However, the vitality of the areas ravaged by bandits has been completely lost. Although they have been reorganized, they have not yet returned to their original state. Therefore, many refugees are still wandering outside, and under the pressure of life, they cannot help but become bandits. Moreover, last year, the Sichuan army was once reduced in size, and the demobilized soldiers did not have a proper occupation, so they could not help but take the path of banditry. Recently, newspapers in Chengdu, Chongqing and other places are full of news about bandits, which shows the prevalence of banditry in various places, and the reason is based on this. Although there are designated pacification zones, relying on unreliable security teams to carry out suppression has little effect. In order to eliminate the bandit atmosphere, the provincial government recently established a Sichuan Rehabilitation and Purging Committee, with Chairman Liu Xiang concurrently serving as the chairman, and Commander Deng Xihou concurrently serving as the vice chairman. The entire province is divided into eleven purging districts, and Chengdu, Chongqing, Wanxian and the three municipalities are designated as special districts. Each district has a commander, who is a brigade commander. Within a short period of time, they are ordered to unite all military police and security teams stationed in the district into a purging force, to undertake the purging, and to combine the strength of the military and the people to jointly eliminate the bandit scourge in the area. After that, there should be no more great difficulties.

Groundless Rumors Arise Frequently

The Department has decided that the defense land left behind by the transfer of the Deng and Sun armies to the Shaanxi-Gansu border will be taken over by which unit, and the authorities have already assigned it. In order to ensure that local security can be permanently maintained, the allocation of stations for the entire Sichuan army must be planned as a whole to avoid uneven distribution of local forces and maintain a balanced state. However, in the situation in Sichuan, whenever there is an extremely ordinary change, rumors arise accordingly. For example, when the Chengdu incident occurred, people generally said that it was directed by someone to deliberately make things difficult for the Central Government, or that someone was sitting idly by and allowing the situation to expand in order to profit from it. A few months ago, there were many rumors about the abnormal movements in Guangxi, and after the overall situation was settled, some people inevitably spread rumors again. Some said that the Central Government would transfer Liu Xiang to lead troops out of Sichuan to garrison somewhere, others said that so-and-so would be transferred to serve as the provincial chairman, and still others said that a certain army would be transferred to garrison in Sichuan Province. In fact, since Chairman Chiang Kai-shek entered Sichuan to reorganize the province last year, the local area and the Central Government have become one. The Central Government has no discriminatory views towards Sichuan, and the Sichuan authorities and military and political leaders are all able to obey the Central Government. Chairman Liu's previous dispatch of Secretary-General Deng Mingjie to fly to Guling to meet Chiang Kai-shek was an even clearer expression. How can there be any resentment between the Central Government and Sichuan Province? Chairman Liu also delivered an important speech at this military affairs conference, saying that since the politics of Sichuan Province have been put on the right track and the entire Sichuan army has been unified, from now on, the strength of Sichuan Province will only follow the instructions of the Central Government and unite with the goal of national salvation. Judging from this, the situation in Sichuan Province is generally known. As for the transfer of the Deng and Sun units, it is only to obey orders to defend against and suppress fleeing bandits. If the bandits are eliminated, they will still be transferred back to their original defenses. In short, the future of Sichuan is focusing on rehabilitation and army reorganization. All rumors are not credible. The people of Shu are prone to rumors, and the ancients have already said it before me. (September 25th)

Completion of the New League of Nations Building; Revival of the Disarmament Committee; Chairman Announces the Start of Debate, but No One Speaks for a Long Time 51

(Geneva) The new League of Nations building, built at a cost of two million pounds, will be officially opened tonight. The Administrative Council will hold a special meeting in it. The new building is extremely magnificent, wider than it is long, with marble walls inlaid with bronze panels. The murals are by the famous Spanish artist Fitte, symbolizing the success of mankind and are extremely eye-catching. The splendor of the ceiling is particularly impressive, with huge statues representing the continents joining hands to maintain peace. (3rd Day Reuters Dispatch)

(Geneva) The opening ceremony of the Administrative Council meeting hall in the new League of Nations building was held at 6:00 PM today. The interior decoration of the meeting hall was designed and arranged by the Catalan artist Maria of Spain, and the Spanish government contributed the funds for the donation. It is extremely magnificent. When the opening ceremony was held today, the Chairman of the Administrative Council and representative of Chile, Rivas, delivered a speech thanking the Spanish government and praising the magnificence of Catalan architecture and art. The Spanish representative, Galardo, then presented the meeting hall to the Administrative Council of the League of Nations in the name of the Spanish government, saying, "This small gift is to express Spain's loyalty to international affairs and its commitment to international regulations." In addition, Bolivia representative Taylor, Swedish representative Sandru, and New Zealand representative Jordan, who were elected as members of the Administrative Council in this session of the League of Nations General Assembly, attended the Administrative Council meeting for the first time today. The Chairman, Rivas, delivered a welcoming speech, and the representatives of the three countries expressed their gratitude. (2nd Day Havas Telegraph)

(Geneva) The Third Committee of the League of Nations General Assembly, the Disarmament Committee, had been suspended since the convening of the Disarmament Conference in 1932 for four years. The League of Nations General Assembly restored it only yesterday. The Committee held its first meeting at 4:00 PM today. Norway representative Launchi was elected as the chairman of the committee, and Turkish representative Satik was elected as the vice chairman. Chairman Launchi first stated the circumstances of the suspension of the Disarmament Conference, saying that the results achieved by the past Disarmament Conference were extremely limited, especially because some of the most relevant countries did not participate, so the work could not help but be suspended. As far as the current situation is concerned, the work of the Disarmament Committee should only be limited to exploring the truth of the disarmament issue for the reference of the League of Nations General Assembly. Afterwards, the General Assembly will notify the Presidium of the Disarmament Conference of the results of this exploration. It seems that nothing else can be done. At this point, the chairman announced the start of the general debate, but no one requested to speak for a long time. Therefore, the Third Committee adjourned the meeting to be reopened tomorrow. (2nd Day Havas Telegraph)

(Geneva) The Administrative Council of the League of Nations held a closed meeting today and decided to temporarily add two non-permanent council seats to the Administrative Council in accordance with the resolution of the League of Nations General Assembly, one of which will be held by China. These two additional non-permanent council seats will be elected by the General Assembly at this session, but the voting date has not yet been determined. (2nd Day Havas Telegraph)

Political Debate 52

(Geneva) The League of Nations General Assembly continued its general debate on political issues at 10:45 this morning. The Chairman, Argentinian Foreign Minister Lamas, invited the Spanish representative, Galardo, to speak first, explaining that the current Spanish government is indeed legitimate, thus refuting the Portuguese representative's earlier speech in the Assembly, where he defined a legitimate government. Galardo stated, "A government is legitimate if it is elected in accordance with the legal principles followed by its people. In the case of the Spanish Republic, the current government has fulfilled all constitutional duties, attended Parliament, and received its confidence. Is this not a legitimate government?" He added that Spain's view of a legitimate government is consistent with the principles upon which the League of Nations is based. Finally, he said, "Some countries, though friends of Spain, have adopted a neutral policy, treating the Spanish rebels and the legitimate government as equals. How can this be?" After his speech, the representatives of Ecuador, Chaldumbide, and Peru, Tudela, delivered speeches in succession. Finally, Chairman Lamas announced the end of the debate. The Assembly then passed a report stipulating that non-League of Nations member states' citizens are eligible for election as judges of the Permanent Court of International Justice in The Hague. It also passed a resolution proposed by the Executive Council, approving the increase of non-permanent members of the Executive Council from nine to eleven, with one seat given to China. At 12:20, the Assembly adjourned. (3rd

The Danzig Question 53

(Geneva) The League of Nations Executive Council previously formed a three-person committee to resolve the dispute in the Free City of Danzig. The committee was originally composed of representatives from the United Kingdom, France, and Portugal. After the current Executive Council meeting, Portugal's term as a member of the Executive Council expired, so Sweden, which was newly elected as a member, took its place. Tonight, the three-person committee, composed of British, French, and Swedish Foreign Ministers Eden, Delbos, and Sandler, met to discuss the situation in the Free City of Danzig. Polish Foreign Minister Beck, with the qualification of being entrusted by the Executive Council to supervise the Free City government, attended the meeting. After discussion, it was decided that Eden would draft a report to be submitted for discussion at the Executive Council's public meeting next Monday. It is reported that the report suggests that Lester should remain as the League of Nations High Commissioner in Danzig until a successor is appointed. Currently, Lester will take a leave of absence for a few weeks and return to Danzig to resume his duties after the vacation. In addition, at the Executive Council meeting next Monday, Poland will be formally entrusted to supervise in order to normalize the relationship between Danzig and the League of Nations. (2nd Havas Dispatch)

Danzig Recent reports suggest that the League of Nations Executive Council is planning to promote High Commissioner Lester to Deputy Secretary-General of the League of Nations and will not send anyone to replace him. Five-Nation Conference 54

(Geneva) French Premier Léon Blum, after arriving in Geneva this morning, met separately with British Foreign Secretary Eden, Romanian Foreign Minister Antonescu, and Soviet Foreign Commissar Litvinov in the afternoon. Tomorrow, he will meet with Polish Foreign Minister Beck and is scheduled to return to Paris the day after tomorrow, Sunday. It is reported that when Léon Blum met with Eden, they discussed three issues: first, whether Anglo-French trade relations could be improved after the devaluation of the French currency; second, the revision of the League of Nations Covenant; and third, the Locarno Five-Nation Conference. According to well-informed sources, the Locarno Five-Nation Conference is unlikely to be convened in the immediate future because there has not been sufficient diplomatic preparation so far. When Romanian Foreign Minister Antonescu met with Premier Léon Blum, he repeatedly reaffirmed Romania's friendship with France and jointly discussed the political and economic issues of the Little Entente countries. Furthermore, according to the Havas correspondent, when Soviet Foreign Commissar Litvinov met with Léon Blum, he repeatedly pointed out that Germany's recent uncompromising attitude towards the Soviet Union has made the Soviet Union extremely uneasy. Therefore, he advocated that all countries that want to safeguard the territorial status quo in Europe should cooperate more closely. (2nd Havas Dispatch)

British Chancellor's Speech: Determination to Expand Armaments; States Air Force is Elite and Invincible; Conservative Party Opposes Foreign Secretary's Overseas Negotiations 55

(London) Chancellor Chamberlain delivered a lengthy speech at the Maelmon Conservative Party Congress today, stating that the British government is proceeding with the rearmament plan, regardless of opposition from any party. Britain's efforts in the disarmament movement are obvious to the world, but because no one has followed Britain's lead, if we do not take steps to make up for our shortcomings, we fear we will not be able to fulfill our responsibilities. Chamberlain continued, "Once the rearmament program is complete, we will once again have a strong navy that can fully protect all lines of communication. Although the army's size cannot be compared with the large-scale conscription of European countries, it will be equipped with the latest weapons and various mechanization methods. At that time, the air force will be second to none in terms of speed, long endurance, engine power, quality, and personnel."

Chamberlain continued, "The development of the world's aviation industry has deprived Britain of some of the benefits of being an island nation. The government has never forgotten the dangers that its people face in times of war, but we must not forget that other countries are far more concerned about such possibilities than we British are. I believe that our air force is the most formidable force in war, so I support its establishment with great faith and enthusiasm, because the world knows that the British air force will never be used for unprovoked wars of aggression."

Chamberlain solemnly declared that the main purpose and desire of the government is to maintain peace. It does not want to seize the territory of others, nor does it intend to interfere in the internal affairs of any other country. The dangers of interfering in the internal affairs of other countries can be seen in the cruelty of the events in Spain. However, thanks to the courageous initiative of French Premier Blum and the support of Britain, the whole of Europe may be divided into two opposing camps. Chamberlain warmly welcomed the establishment of the London International Committee. The British government believes that the establishment of regional agreements within the League of Nations Covenant will materially consolidate the prospect of world peace, because under this agreement, countries with major interests can mutually guarantee to resolve well-known dispute areas. The British government intends to negotiate a public agreement with Western Europe.

Referring to the British Empire, Chamberlain stated that even if there are various difficulties in the interpretation of the Ottawa Agreement, there are indeed considerable provisions in it so that both parties can begin to exchange views. Chamberlain believes that the harmony of opinions among the governments of the various autonomous territories and the British Imperial government on various common interests, foreign policy, defense, and trade has never been greater than in the four years since the Ottawa Treaty was signed. Chamberlain then declared that Prime Minister Baldwin hopes to be able to meet all the heavy responsibilities of the present when Parliament reopens.

Before the adjournment, a resolution was passed urging the government to change its policy of successive foreign ministers usurping the responsibilities of competent ambassadors for the sake of world peace. The motion criticized the impropriety of the foreign minister personally going abroad to discuss international affairs and solemnly declared that this proposal was not aimed at Foreign Secretary Eden personally. (2nd Reuters Dispatch)

(London) The Labor Party Executive Committee held a meeting in Edinburgh City yesterday, and after discussing it all day, it finally passed a resolution, stating that "the current government is unable to fulfill the promises it has made to maintain peace, and the Party can only continue to work hard to impeach it and promote the Party's positive international policy with all its strength so as to regain power." (3rd Havas Dispatch)

France Reduces Tariffs: Raw Materials Reduced by 20%, Finished Products Reduced by 15%; Effective from October 10th 56

(Paris) The government previously imposed additional taxes on imported goods from certain countries due to the imbalance of foreign exchange rates in order to remedy the situation. Now, because the devaluation policy of the French franc has taken effect, it issued an order this morning stipulating that the additional taxes should be reduced or abolished from October 10th. Among them, the additional taxes on goods imported from China and Japan have been reduced from 15% to 10%. The additional taxes on goods from Australia, Egypt, India, New Zealand, Paraguay, Argentina, and the Union of South Africa have been completely abolished. In addition, the government has issued several orders to reduce tariffs in order to gradually achieve a free trade policy, namely (1) raw materials not subject to import quotas are reduced by 20%, semi-finished products are reduced by 17%, and finished products are reduced by 15%; (2) all goods within import quotas are reduced by 20%; (3) a special tariff committee is established to study (a) methods for further reducing tariffs, and (b) abolishing import quotas when prices rise excessively. Government officials claim that after the tariff reduction, prices can be reduced by 3% to 5%. (3rd Havas Dispatch)

Austrian Home Guard: Two Giants in Unresolved Dispute 58

(Vienna) The leader of the Vienna Province Patriotic Home Guard was originally Chief of the former Ministry of Interior, Major Fey. The leaders of various branches across the country held a meeting yesterday to discuss the matter. The members resolved unanimously to expel Major Fey and Vienna Deputy Mayor Rahl from the group and issued a public statement in the evening explaining the reasons for this decision, stating that Major Fey and Rahl stood in opposition within the Patriotic Home Guard, and Major Fey was particularly concerned with undermining the unity of the group, and Fey's position when former Prime Minister Dollfuss was murdered on July 25th of the previous year was also vague and has always been a source of suspicion. This is the reason for the expulsion of Fey and Rahl. In addition, Prince Starhemberg has also issued a decree to all members, especially members of the Vienna Province branch, forbidding them from associating with Major Fey, otherwise they will be expelled. Fey also plans to expel Prince Starhemberg from the Vienna Province branch in retaliation. It is now known that the Patriotic Home Guard discussed the murder of former Prime Minister Dollfuss when it met yesterday. Therefore, the above public statement mentioned this matter, but at the last minute, the newspapers in the capital received an order from the police authorities not to reprint it. From this point of view, Chancellor Schuschnigg seems to be not standing idly by in the dispute between Starhemberg and Fey. (2nd Havas Dispatch)

Paris Café Strike: Hotels and Taverns Also Join 59

(Paris) The hotels, taverns, and cafes in this city went on strike this morning. On the Champs-Élysées and other major streets, most of the shops have joined the strike, except for a few shops where labor and management have reached an agreement. When the market opened this morning, the tables and chairs in front of the taverns and cafes were moved away. In front of most hotels in the central district, there were pickets stationed to monitor. However, some hotel authorities took precautions in advance, so they were not affected by the strike. Generally, the striking waiters stayed put, and the police went to the Champs-Élysées first to persuade them to withdraw, and they all expressed obedience and there were no disturbances. The police are now going to other areas to persuade them. The government previously made a promise in the Senate that when striking workers stay in the workplace, it must do its best to stop them. Premier Léon Blum also reiterated this when debating the new currency bill in the House of Representatives. This is the first time that the above promise has been put into practice. (3rd Havas Dispatch)

Current Commentary

The Highest Limit of Diplomatic Efforts 62

— Hua

For over a month, the diplomatic relations between China and Japan have been trending towards tension step by step, reaching the most serious stage in the recent ten days or so. The creation of this situation is superficially due to two reasons. The first is the so-called "unfortunate incidents" that occurred successively in Chengdu, Beihai, Hankou, and Shanghai. The Japanese side did not take a calm attitude to investigate the fundamental causes, but instead fueled the flames, using them to coerce the Chinese authorities, resulting in an unexpectedly tense situation. The second is the negotiations in Nanjing between our Foreign Minister Zhang and Japanese Ambassador Kawagoe. Due to the disparity of opinions, they could not progress smoothly, and the unreasonable demands of the Japanese side transmitted by Reuters and the hard-line attitude of Tokyo shown by the Domei News Agency have all made the Chinese people feel angry and uneasy. These two situations, especially the Japanese side's deliberate ostentation and fierce stimulation after the Hongkou incident, have created an extraordinary atmosphere, making us feel that the "adjustment" of Sino-Japanese relations has indeed reached a critical juncture on the diplomatic path.

However, at such a serious juncture, according to the verbal statements of the Japanese side, they have not yet abandoned the determination to take the diplomatic route. A telegram from Tokyo yesterday reported that the Ministry of Foreign Affairs has dispatched the Director of the East Asia Bureau, Kuwajima, to China with a concrete proposal decided by the three-ministry conference to convey it to Ambassador Kawagoe, preparing to reopen negotiations. It seems that in the very bleak current situation, there is still a glimmer of hope for a "turn for the better." However, we must point out that we do not have excessive illusions about this statement from the Japanese side. We will certainly not refuse to resolve Sino-Japanese problems through diplomatic channels, but "adjusting" the relations between the two countries diplomatically must follow the proper path and must not violate the basic stance of an independent country. Leaving these two points means exceeding the highest limit of diplomatic efforts. We absolutely cannot tolerate it. We would like to take advantage of the current serious moment to explain our views on diplomacy.

First, fundamentally, we should recognize that the abnormality of Sino-Japanese relations began at least in 1931, at the time of the "September 18th Incident," and was definitely not caused by some recent incidents. The occupation of many places such as the three eastern provinces, Rehe, eastern Hebei, and northern Chahar, the bombing of the flourishing city of Shanghai, the carrying out of the puppet autonomy movement, and the rampant armed smuggling, these major incidents are truly "incomparable" when compared with some recent incidents. The accounts should be settled from the beginning. In the current diplomatic negotiations, we must make a whole clearance with the other side for the damage to our country's territorial sovereignty over the past five years.

Second, in the course of the abnormality of Sino-Japanese relations over the past five years, we have seen that the Japanese side only has force and no diplomacy towards China. If there is any, it is diplomacy under the bayonet. Therefore, we believe that the negotiations on the Shanghai Ceasefire Agreement, the Tanggu Truce, and the He-Umezu Agreement were not conducted under normal diplomacy. Now, if the Japanese side is indeed sincere in conducting negotiations through proper diplomatic channels, we should naturally demand the abolition of these agreements. Moreover, in the past, the Japanese side often deliberately targeted local authorities in many negotiations with our country, failing to follow the normal diplomatic channels. At present, the Japanese side insists on abandoning the proper channel of negotiating with Foreign Minister Zhang and demands so-called "direct" negotiations with President Jiang of the Executive Yuan. It is even more evident that the arrogant attitude of a group of Japanese military officers last year has not changed to this day. Such means of not following the normal diplomatic track will certainly not bring Sino-Japanese diplomatic relations into the proper path.

Third, the demands made by the Japanese side in the Nanjing negotiations have been published by Reuters based on news from the Tokyo "Yomiuri Shimbun," namely the four items regarding the "autonomy" of the five provinces in North China, the Sino-Japanese transport agreement, the further reduction of Chinese tariffs on Japanese goods, and the use of Japanese advisors as much as possible. The essence of these four demands is to completely turn China into a colony of Japan. However, the other day, the spokesman of the Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Amau, suddenly published an article attacking Reuters, calling such news "fantastic propaganda." True, although we dare not determine whether these demands are true, we dare to assert that these demands are not only fantastic but also utterly absurd. All demands that harm China's territorial sovereignty are absurd "fantasies" that exceed the highest limit of Sino-Japanese diplomatic efforts.

Finally, we should also frankly state that the Chinese people do not have any excessive "illusions" about Japan. We only have one legitimate demand, which is to restore our territory and sovereignty. In order to protect China's territory and sovereignty, we are not afraid of any sacrifice.

Spanish Rebel Leader: Franco Implements Dictatorship, Announces Provisional Government Organization Law, Advocates Catholicism and Preserves National Essence 63

Burgos - General Franco, Commander-in-Chief of the Spanish rebel forces, today announced the organization of the new government via radio from here to the world, stating that Spain will establish a new political situation based on dictatorship. It will comprehensively consider traditional customs, national welfare, national unity, and historical evolution. The government will also advocate Catholicism, give preferential treatment to countries with the same language and culture, and maintain friendly relations with all countries, except Soviet Russia. After Franco's speech, he immediately ordered the implementation of a dictatorship and the establishment of a provisional State Council. The State Council will be composed of the Chairman of the Technical Committee, the Governors of the recovered provinces, the Director of the Government Secretariat, the Minister of Foreign Affairs, the Minister of Finance, the Minister of Justice, the Minister of Industry, the Minister of Agriculture and Forestry, the Minister of Labor, the Minister of Education, the Minister of Public Works, and the Minister of Transportation. Their names have not yet been announced. (National Telegram, 2nd)

Burgos - Following his inauguration yesterday, General Franco, head of the National Army Government, immediately convened a State Council meeting. After the meeting, he issued an order to regulate the organization and powers of the National Army Government. It stated that the National Army Government would establish a State Council, under which would be seven specialized committees: (1) Finance Committee, (2) Justice Committee, (3) Industry and Commerce Committee, (4) Agriculture Committee, (5) Labor Committee, (6) Education Committee, and (7) Construction Committee. In addition, a Ministry of Foreign Affairs will be established to oversee propaganda matters. All laws and decrees must be reviewed by the respective specialized committees and then submitted to the head of the National Army Government through the State Council for approval before taking effect. The governors of the provinces currently controlled by the National Army have also been appointed by General Franco. General Cabanellas, former Chairman of the Military Government, has been appointed Inspector General of Army Education, General Mola has been reappointed Commander of the Northern Front, and General Dávila has been promoted to Commander of the Southern Front. (Havas Telegram, 3rd)

Lisbon - General Franco, commander of the Spanish rebel forces, today issued a declaration to the Spanish people, stating that the new Spain will follow Portugal's example and implement a corporatist system. He absolutely guaranteed to secure work for all the people, no longer subject to the shackles of capitalism, and would stipulate a minimum wage. All the rights previously obtained by workers will be respected, but the general "parasites" in society will be eliminated. As for the Roman Catholic Church, it will establish harmonious coordination with the government. (Reuters Telegram, 3rd)

Burgos - Since being elected as "Head of State of Spain," General Francisco Franco, Commander-in-Chief of the National Army, will set up his office in the old Provincial Council in the city of Burgos. Last night, after taking office, General Franco broadcast a speech on the Castile radio station, expressing his political views. According to the political views of the Spanish government army, it can be divided into two factions: one faction is the Carlist royalists who support the Carlos dynasty (note: Prince Carlos, the heir to the Carlos dynasty, died in a car accident in Vienna a few days ago), advocating the restoration of autocratic monarchy. Whether the king represents divine power is yet to be determined. In terms of social organization, they advocate a family system. This faction, led by Fal Conde, is smaller in number but has a strong cohesion. The other faction is the Falangist fascists belonging to the Falange Española de las JONS. This faction's political program was drafted by the son of the former dictator Rivera, the leader of the Falange, and is based on the Italian fascist system, advocating the establishment of a vocational group state. The political views of these two factions often conflict. The political program announced by General Franco this time is a compromise between the views of the two factions. In the first half of his speech, he advocated that the government adopt an authoritarian system centered on the military. Although local autonomy will be respected, it will be limited to not weakening national power. As for the question of whether to restore the monarchy, it will be decided by the people through vocational group organizations in the future. This proposition is obviously intended to satisfy the Carlist royalists. However, in the second half of his speech, he advocated protecting the interests of workers, preventing excessive capitalism, workers should receive fair remuneration, and participate in profit sharing, but must cooperate loyally with the "wealthy." All Spaniards should work according to their abilities, and all parasitic classes are not tolerated by the new government. All of the above is obviously to satisfy the requirements of the Fascist Party. In addition, whether Catholicism should become the state religion according to the royalist proposal, Franco did not reveal in his speech. He only stated that the government should decide its attitude towards the Catholic Church based on the religious situation of the majority of the Spanish people. Regarding the land issue, Franco only stated that the new government should protect family hereditary property, improve land use, and ensure fair remuneration for agricultural products. Finally, General Franco said that Spain is willing to cooperate with the people of all countries in harmony, but refuses to cooperate with countries that adopt a communist system. As for the people of South American countries with the same language and culture as Spain, the new government should especially find ways to maintain closer spiritual and material relations with the Spanish people. (Havas Telegram, 2nd)

Madrid: Conspiracy Cracked; Foreign Minister Re-announces Italian and German Aid to Rebels 65

Madrid - Three hundred members of the Catholic Action Party were secretly meeting today when they were surrounded by the capital's police and two hundred people were arrested. They planned to occupy the capital with 40 aircraft and 3,000 rebel soldiers. (National Telegram, 2nd)

(Geneva) - The Spanish delegation to the League of Nations also released several documents last night to prove that Italy and Germany have repeatedly violated the non-intervention agreement in the civil war. (1) The German cargo ship "Chevalier," ostensibly carrying coal, was transported to the international neutral port of Tangier in Africa, but in fact, the coal was hiding munitions, which had arrived at the port of Melilla (rebel base in Spanish Morocco) on the 29th of last month. (2) Italy supplied the rebels with poison gas and arms on the 27th of last month. (3) On the same day, twelve German giant bombers were transported to the port of Tangier and were immediately deployed, carrying several rebels from Tetouan, Morocco, to Seville in mainland Spain. (4) The Italian gunboat "Ariaconda" departed from Trieste and arrived near the port of Tetouan on the 12th of last month, immediately unloading poison gas, aircraft, bombs and munitions to supply the rebels. The above are only the main points; there are countless others. (Havas Telegram, 2nd)

(New York) - Literary magazines today released another public opinion poll on the presidential election. However, adding up the previous numbers, Landon still received 438,601 votes, while President Roosevelt received 282,524 votes. According to this poll, Landon received the most votes in 290 election districts in Arizona, California, Idaho, Illinois, Indiana, Iowa, Kansas, Maine, Michigan, Minnesota, Nebraska, New Jersey, New York, North Dakota, Ohio, Oregon, Pennsylvania, Montana, South Dakota, and Washington. Roosevelt had an advantage in 111 election districts in the South, including Arkansas, Florida, Georgia, Louisiana, Mississippi, Missouri, Oklahoma, Texas, and Utah. Compared with the Republican and Democratic parties, the votes received by candidates from smaller parties were insignificant. Union Party candidate Lemke received a total of 29,038 votes, Socialist Party candidate Thomas received 3,343 votes, and Communist Party candidate Browder received only 1,523 votes. (National Telegram, 2nd)

I have publicly stated in the Senate that in order to relieve the poor and helpless, I would vote in favor of using up all the national treasury." Democratic leader Smith just delivered a speech yesterday, expressing his support for Republican presidential candidate Landon, and Republican heavyweight Borah came out today to support the Democratic Party, which shocked the general public. (Havas Telegram, 2nd)

Tianjin Municipality Begins Collecting Income Tax; Banks Have Not Received Detailed Procedures; Municipal Agencies Start Collection as Scheduled 70

Tianjin Correspondence: The implementation of the income tax here can be described in three parts. Regarding the collection of income tax on interest from bonds and deposits by the three major banks (Bank of China, Bank of Communications, and Central Bank) and other banks, money shops, and silver firms, the Central Bank had only received the Ministry of Finance's general tax collection outline as of the 1st. The detailed implementation rules had not yet been received. Other banks had not received instructions from their Shanghai headquarters, so all procedures were unclear. Li Da, the former manager of the Central Bank in Tianjin, was transferred to Shanghai. Before receiving the transfer order, he was entrusted by the Tianjin banks and money shops to go to Shanghai to negotiate. However, the transfer order was recently announced, and his successor, Bian Chucheng, has not yet taken office. It seems that no one is responsible in the banking sector. However, because the Ministry of Finance's "Income Tax Collection Guidelines" contains four rules, each bank has an absolute obligation and cannot delay. Therefore, on the 1st, they sent telegrams one after another, requesting their Shanghai headquarters to send the procedures as soon as possible to facilitate the start. It is rumored that the Ministry of Finance will send personnel north to supervise implementation within the next week. According to the banking community, it is necessary to clearly understand how the tax payments will be remitted after the income tax is collected so that the process will not be delayed. The issue of clearing deposits and bond interest is not a problem, as each bank has monthly settlements. Although the procedures are cumbersome, there are no major difficulties.

Regarding the collection of income tax from civil servants, the municipal government ordered all its subordinate agencies on September 28 to pay the tax on October 1 in accordance with the regulations issued by the central government. It would be deducted from their salaries each month when they were paid by the heads of the respective agencies. Ma Yanzhong, Secretary-General of the Tianjin Municipal Government, also stated that the central government's intention to collect income tax is upright, and the people should bear it so that small amounts can be collected into large amounts to help the national treasury. The Tianjin Municipal Government will implement it as scheduled without any difficulty. The municipality has been collecting income donations for many years. After the income tax is collected, the donation will be stopped at the same time. However, it is difficult to guarantee that agencies outside the municipal government will comply as scheduled.

Regarding free professional groups, most of them are still waiting, as they do not fully understand this move. The supervision and promotion of the official is more important. The Municipal Chamber of Commerce, which has been greatly affected by commercial depression and smuggling, has been suffering from poor returns in all industries. Based on the early requests of more than 90 trade associations, it forwarded a request to the Ministry of Finance to postpone the tax collection. The Ministry of Finance has not yet replied. Because tax collection is starting, the Chamber of Commerce convened a meeting of various trade associations on the afternoon of the 2nd to discuss how to proceed. On the morning of the 5th, another meeting of the Tianjin Municipal Chamber of Commerce Reorganization Committee will be convened, with the results of the 2nd day's meeting as the purpose of discussion. It will be submitted to the central government again, urging it to understand the desolation of North China's commerce and the hardship of the merchants, and to provide consideration, exempting them from the immediate tax collection. It would not be too late to start collecting when the market is slightly more active. In addition, various groups located in the concessions are protected by special forces and have not paid attention to this matter at all, so promotion is even more impossible. (1st)

Guangdong Merchants Appeal for the Maintenance of Previously Suspended Banknotes; Former Provincial Bank Notes and Old Central 10 Yuan Notes; Total Amount of Suspended Banknotes is Approximately 20 Million Yuan 71

Guangzhou Correspondence: Guangdong merchants recently learned that the government will issue 120 million yuan of public bonds to reorganize Guangdong's finances, and Zhong E was sent south to prepare for the establishment of a branch of the Central Bank in Guangdong. A preparatory office has recently been established, and the branch address has been selected in the Thirteenth Hongs in Xiguan. This shows that the central government has concrete measures to reorganize Guangdong's finances and currency system. However, it was found that when the Central Bank was previously established in Guangdong, it issued a 10-yuan banknote in Guangdong. After the Central Bank moved north, it stopped redeeming it. The number of Central Bank banknotes that stopped redemption and remained in the Guangdong market was very large. So far, it has only become a commodity. Because of the suspension of redemption, its value is only 60-70% of the current Guangdong silver coins. (That is, 10 yuan of Central Bank banknotes that stopped redemption are worth 6-7 yuan of silver. However, the market price is different, and it has recently been higher than before.) Merchants who hold these banknotes have suffered great losses. Therefore, various firms jointly wrote to the Guangzhou Municipal Chamber of Commerce, forwarding a request to the government authorities to maintain them. Taking advantage of this period of reorganizing Guangdong's currency system, they should quickly recover the Central Bank banknotes that have stopped redemption at full value. The Municipal Chamber of Commerce believes that this move has a great impact on the financial circulation of merchants, and especially proposed it for discussion at the 14th meeting on the 29th. It was then decided to forward the joint request of the city's velvet money industry and other five trade associations to the government to recover the suspended banknotes in Guangdong Province at full value as soon as possible. The details of the case are as follows: (1) The old Guangdong Provincial Bank banknotes were issued by Sun Yat-sen when he returned to Guangdong to govern in December 15th of the Republic of China's 9th year. On May 5th of the 10th year, after Sun Yat-sen took the position of Extraordinary President, he led his troops on the Northern Expedition. Due to the huge military expenses, more than 17 million yuan was misappropriated from the bank. The bank's fund was empty, and a run occurred. On February 8th of the 12th year, it was announced that it would stop circulation. In March of the same year, the Grand Marshal ordered the Finance Department to set up a banknote clearing office to engage in clearing. By September, he repeatedly ordered the former Chief of Finance of the Grand Marshal's Headquarters, Ye Gongchuo, and the Governor of Guangdong Province, Xu Shaozhen, Liao Zhongkai, and others to try to maintain it. After the establishment of the National Government, the Minister of Finance, Song, issued a statement when clearing the Bank of China banknotes, stating that he would continue to clear the Guangdong Bank banknotes of the provincial bank. Merchants were deeply hopeful, but because the political situation was not yet unified, it has not been implemented. (2) The old 10-yuan banknotes of Guangdong Bank were issued after the reorganization of the Central Bank in the 18th year. In April of the 20th year, they were suspended due to political changes. In January of the 20th year, the provincial government reorganized the bank into Guangdong Provincial Bank, and successively recovered various Bank of China banknotes. Only this 10-yuan banknote remains, because the number of issues is relatively large, and it has not been recovered yet. Now that the Guangdong situation has been stabilized, the above-mentioned two types of suspended banknotes are only more than 20 million yuan. The government can announce their maintenance on a specific day. However, merchants have been waiting quietly until now, and have not heard of any practical measures. Therefore, they especially described the past losses of the merchants and appealed for the forwarding of the request to the authorities to quickly provide maintenance and relief. (September 30th)

Recent Developments in Sichuan Highways 72

Chengdu Correspondence: Sichuan's highway trunk lines, whether completed, uncompleted, or under planning, collectively encompass the routes of Sichuan-Guizhou, Sichuan-Shaanxi, Sichuan-Hunan, Sichuan-Hubei, Sichuan-Xikang, Sichuan-Gansu, Sichuan-Qinghai, the Central Route of Sichuan-Yunnan, the Eastern Route of Sichuan-Yunnan, and the Western Route of Sichuan-Yunnan. All ten major trunk lines are centered in Chengdu. The recent conditions of the completed routes, the progress of the uncompleted routes, and a summary of the planned routes under preparation are described separately below.

A. Completed Trunk Lines:

(1) Sichuan-Guizhou Route: Starting from the Niushikou Station outside the East Gate of Chengdu, passing through Chongqing to the Chongxi River at the border of Sichuan and Guizhou, this is the Sichuan section of the route. From the Chongxi River, it passes through Songkan, Tongzi, and Zunyi, directly reaching Guiyang, which is the Guizhou section of the route. The entire route is 979 kilometers long. The entire road is now open to traffic. It takes one and a half days to travel from Chengdu to Chongqing, and one day from Chongqing to Songkan. The operation of vehicles and business are entirely managed by the Sichuan Highway Bureau, eliminating the various malpractices of private car companies in the past. Travelers praise the convenience. Recently, the Highway Bureau conducted a major autumn review of the Sichuan-Guizhou route to inspect the business conditions along the route, the status of vehicles, the suitability of station setups, and whether station staff are competent. The review was led by Bureau Chief Wei Junfan and Advisor Xu Xingcheng, along with the heads of various departments and sections of the bureau. They departed from Chengdu by car on September 26th. Lei Baohua, Director of the Shaanxi Construction Department, who was in Chengdu on official business, also accompanied the inspection. The group was scheduled to return to Chengdu on October 5th. The trip was divided into four groups. The first group, which departed on the 26th, included Central News Agency reporter Huang Jingnan. They arrived in Chongqing on the 27th. The remaining three groups departed over the following four days. After gathering in Chongqing, they proceeded together to Songkan, which was the final destination of the inspection. Director Wei scheduled a meeting on the 28th to address the staff stationed in Chongqing. According to Wei, the inspection results along the way were very good, but a final evaluation would be made after the second group completed its review.

(2) Sichuan-Shaanxi Route: Starting from the Boji Street Station outside the North Gate of Chengdu, passing through Xindu, Guanghan, Deyang, Luojiang, Mianyang, Zitong, Jiange, Zhaohua, Guangyuan, and ending in Ningqiang, Shaanxi Province, the entire route is 412 kilometers long. The section from Chengdu to Mianyang was built in the past, but the work was perfunctory, and the roadbed deteriorated early. From October 1935 to February 1936, construction was carried out to reorganize and complete the section, making it relatively smooth. The construction of the section from Mianyang to Ningqiang was extremely difficult, with a budget of 1,645,000 yuan allocated from the Sichuan Rehabilitation Public Bonds by the Field Headquarters. The entire route was completed by the end of May this year, and a trial opening to traffic was held on June 1st. The operation of vehicles and business are entirely managed by the Sichuan Highway Bureau. Regarding the joint operation agreement for the Sichuan-Shaanxi route, it was signed by Sichuan Highway Bureau Chief Wei Junfan on September 17th during a trip to Shaanxi, with Zeng Xiangwu, Director of the Northwest National Highway Administration. It is expected to be officially opened to traffic in early November. Currently, north of Jiange in Sichuan Province, the roadbed has not been properly repaired, making driving extremely difficult. In addition, banditry is rampant in Mianyang, Luojiang, Zitong, and other counties, and robberies of cars occur frequently. As a result, the automobile business performance on this route is far less than that of the Chengdu-Chongqing section of the Sichuan-Guizhou route.

B. Uncompleted Trunk Lines:

(1) Sichuan-Hunan Route: Starting from Gongjiang on the Sichuan-Guizhou route, passing through Nanchuan, Pengshui, Qianjiang, Youyang, and Xiushan, and ending at Chashan Town at the border of Sichuan and Hunan, the route is 704 kilometers long. Qijiang County started construction at the end of November last year, and the entire line started construction at the end of January this year. The total construction cost is estimated at over 4,346,000 yuan, allocated from the Sichuan Rehabilitation Public Bonds by the Field Headquarters. The progress of the entire route's work has been quite slow. As of the end of August, the road surface completion rate was 24% for the Qijiang to Pengshui section and 10% for the Qianjiang to Xiushan section. The Military Affairs Commission's Field Headquarters specifically instructed the Sichuan Provincial Government to issue orders to the Highway Bureau and the county governments along the Sichuan-Hunan route, using extremely stern language, stating that "The Hunan section of the Sichuan-Hunan highway has been completely opened to traffic by the end of August. The Sichuan section is hereby ordered to be fully open to traffic by the end of October, without further delay. The provincial government must strictly order the county governments along the route to comply diligently and intensify their work. Any delay will be severely punished without leniency." The Hunan section of this route starts from the aforementioned Chashan Town, passes through Yongshui, Qiancheng, and Luxi, and ends at Shaojiwan, connecting to the completed Xiang-Qian highway, directly reaching Changsha. This section is 200 kilometers long, which is two-thirds shorter than the Sichuan section, hence the rapid opening to traffic.

(2) Sichuan-Hubei Route: This route starts from the Jianyang Station on the Chengdu-Chongqing section of the Sichuan-Guizhou route, passes through Lezhi, Suining, Pengxi, Nanchong, Yuechi, Guang'an, Qu County, Dazhu, Liangshan, and Wanxian, crosses the Yangtze River, and reaches Lichuan County in Hubei Province. The entire route is 809 kilometers long. The Jian-Qu section, 470 kilometers long, is open to traffic. The section from Qu County to the Dazhu Watershed, 187 kilometers long, has 30% of the road surface completed as of the end of August, while the remaining stone and bridge culvert projects have been completed. The section from Wanxian across the Yangtze River to Lichuan in Hubei Province has not yet started construction. It is reported that the Highway Supervision Office of the Field Headquarters has recently decided to build only to Wanxian and to open another route from Qianjiang Station on the Sichuan-Hunan route to Xianfeng in Hubei Province, 25 kilometers long, to connect with the highway from Xianfeng to Badong.

(3) Sichuan-Xikang Route: Starting from the station outside the South Gate of Chengdu, passing through Shuangliu, Xinjin, Qionglai, Mingshan, Ya'an, Tianquan, Luding, and ending in Kangding (Dajianlu) in Xikang, the entire route is 373 kilometers long. The Chengdu-Ya'an section, 173 kilometers long, was built in the past and is already open to traffic. The Ya'an to Kangding section has steep mountains and is difficult to construct. Although construction has started, it is feared that it will be difficult to complete within the year.

C. Planned Trunk Lines:

(1) Sichuan-Gansu Route: According to the Highway Bureau's plan, it is proposed to start from the Zhaohua Station on the Sichuan-Shaanxi route, pass through Baoningyuan, and reach Bikou in Gansu. The entire route is 100 kilometers long, which is very short. However, Zhaohua, Guangyuan, Langzhong, and other places have not yet recovered from bandit disturbances, making it difficult to recruit labor and soldiers. Troops passing through often engage in forced conscription. The date of construction of this route is still far off.

(2) Sichuan-Qinghai Route: Also one of the planned trunk lines, it is proposed to start from Mianyang Station on the Sichuan-Shaanxi route, pass through Zhangming, Jiangyou, Pingwu, Songpan, and enter Qinghai at Suogezang Temple. The entire route is 552 kilometers long. Currently, only the 53-kilometer road from Mianyang to Jiangyou has been built. However, bandits along the way are rampant and unscrupulous, and car drivers are wary, and passengers dare not take risks, all detouring. The section from Jiangyou to Suogezang Temple has not yet been surveyed, and it is unknown when construction will begin.

(3) Central Route of Sichuan-Yunnan: According to the highway plan for the trunk line from Sichuan to Yunnan, it is proposed to build three routes: central, eastern, and western. The construction cost is estimated to require more than 6,600,000 yuan, and a request has been submitted to the Field Headquarters for allocation from the construction public bonds. First, the central route plan is described: starting from Xinjin County on the Sichuan-Xikang route, reaching Pengshan, Meishan, Jiajiang, Leshan, Jianwei, and Pingshan, and reaching Yibin at the border of Sichuan and Yunnan, the entire route is 320 kilometers long. The section from Xinjin to Wutongqiao in Jianwei, 142 kilometers long, and the section from Jianwei to Qingshui Creek, 15 kilometers long, were built early. The remaining sections have not yet been built.

(4) Eastern Route of Sichuan-Yunnan: Starting from Longchang, passing through Luxian, Naxi, Xuyong, and reaching Chishui River at the border of Sichuan and Yunnan, the entire route is 250 kilometers long. Currently, only the section from Xuyong to Jiangmenchang, 40 kilometers long, has been completed. The rest is under survey.

(5) Western Route of Sichuan-Yunnan: Starting from Luding on the Sichuan-Xikang route, passing through Mianning, Xichang, and Huili, and reaching Pulong Town, the entire route is 600 kilometers long. No survey has been conducted yet. In total, the three Sichuan-Yunnan routes have no significant progress. Recently, the entire Yunnan-Guizhou highway has been completed, with traffic from Kunming to Guiyang, and then from Guiyang to Chongqing, indirectly benefiting Sichuan-Yunnan transportation, which is also of great importance. In mid-September, Qiu Chuanmeng, Secretary of the Highway Office of the Field Headquarters, and 10 others were sent to test drive, departing from Guiyang and arriving in Kunming in three days. They then discussed joint operations with the Yunnan Highway Bureau, intending to imitate the methods of the five provinces of Jiangsu and Zhejiang and establish regulations for joint automobile transportation in the five provinces of Sichuan, Yunnan, Guizhou, Hunan, and Guangxi to jointly promote development. The completion of the Yunnan-Guizhou highway not only facilitates the transportation of passengers and goods between Sichuan and Yunnan but also forms a transportation network for the five southwestern provinces, which is sufficient to open a new era in history. From Kunming to Panxian, transfer to Guiyang, reach Chongqing, and then connect to the Sichuan-Yunnan road to reach Changsha, which can be implemented within this year. The Field Headquarters is urging the Sichuan Provincial Government to complete the Sichuan-Hunan trunk line within a limited time for the sake of implementing the five-province joint transportation plan.

Suzhou 73

Establishment of a Land Ownership Representative Group

The original organization of the city and rural land owners in this county, called the Taxpayer Assembly (initially called the Land Ownership Association), is now proposed to be reorganized into the Land Ownership Association. Upon submission to the County Magistrate, it was approved to be renamed the Land Ownership Representative Group. On the afternoon of the second day at 2:00 PM, a general meeting of more than 270 owners and representatives from the city and countryside was convened. The presidium reported the purpose of reorganizing the Land Ownership Representative Group and then discussed and elected the representatives of the Representative Group, stipulating a quota of 27 people. In addition to the warehouse association, the relief agency, and the property management office as ex officio representatives, 13 people including Wu Boyin were elected from the city, and 11 people including Yan Kangbo were elected from the countryside, totaling 27 people to form the Land Ownership Representative Group. Subsequently, various proposals were discussed. Regarding the cases of reported wasteland in Xiangcheng and other places, it was decided to send 38 industry stalls to the countryside for investigation. Hereafter, the name of the Land Ownership Assembly will no longer be used internally or externally, but the name of the Land Ownership Representative Group will be used.

Morphine Criminals Escorted to Province for Trial

The Public Security Bureau previously transferred two morphine traffickers, Zhang Boliang and Zhang Lansheng, who were seized by the Third Branch Bureau while operating outside. After interrogation, they were transferred to the County Government for review. The County Government, considering that the case involved trafficking in narcotics, which should be handled by military law, dispatched detectives yesterday (the 3rd) at 7:00 or 8:00 AM to escort the two criminals to the Zhenjiang Garrison Command for trial.

Jiading 74

Notorious Native Opium Trafficker Arrested

At 9:00 PM on the 30th of last month, the Shanghai-Xianghu train arrived in Nanxiang. Zhang Sanbao, a resident of Zhuangjiajing, Shanghai County, purchased 80 taels of Yunnan opium and 25 taels of Sichuan opium in Shanghai. His demeanor was flustered when he got off the train. Wuxi 75

Silk Cocoon Merchants Telegraph Province for Assistance

Chen Xiekun, Chairman of the Joint Association of Silk Cocoon Industry Associations of Jiangsu Province, Hua Shaochun, Chairman of the Silk Cocoon Industry Association of Wuxi, Qian Fenghao, Chairman of the Silk Factory Industry Association, and others stated that the autumn silkworms in this province suffered from poor development and reduced harvests because the seed acid immersion date was too early and coincided with adverse weather. The quality of cocoons varied greatly. The Jiangsu Provincial Sericulture Improvement Association uniformly referred to the cocoons as being of excellent quality, regardless of their actual quality. Initially, the price of cocoons was set at 29 yuan per dan as a balancing standard, but later it was stipulated that the price per dan should not be lower than 29 yuan, otherwise, strict penalties would be imposed. Silk cocoon merchants engage in the silk cocoon business, hoping to win glory for China's foreign trade, which is not comparable to ordinary commercial activities for pure profit. Over the years, they have suffered huge losses due to the influence of overseas markets, and they are now bankrupt and struggling to survive. The cocoon price set by the Sericulture Improvement Association is appropriate, but whether the initially set balancing standard of 29 yuan or the later minimum price of 29 yuan is more appropriate is unclear. The government automatically changes orders in the morning and revokes them in the evening. Merchants have repeatedly telegraphed for relief, stating that they should consult widely. For the sake of the lifeline of silk farmers and silk merchants throughout Jiangsu Province, they specifically jointly telegraphed the Jiangsu Construction Department and the Sericulture Improvement Management Committee yesterday to request assistance.

Half-Decomposed Corpse Found Hanging in Yi County

On a cypress tree in the ancestral grave of Yu Lin's family on Dongguan Community Mountain in the middle section of Jin Yuan Road from Meiyuan to Xiaojishan in the Fourth District of the county, an unidentified male corpse was found hanging this morning. The corpse was wearing a white undershirt, and the head had become a skeleton with only a few strands of hair remaining. The muscles of the upper body, except for most of the rotted parts, had been air-dried. The lower half of the corpse, from the chest down, including both hands and the intestines and lungs inside the abdomen, had been eaten by wild animals. The two wrist bones protruded. There were many body fragments on the ground, along with a pair of twill cloth single shoes. There were many wild animal claw marks on the cypress tree. The sight was terrifying. It is expected that the corpse committed suicide more than a month ago. Shan Hongyuan, the head of the Nian San Yi Tu, learned of the situation and reported it to the local court, requesting an inquest. Prosecutor Shen Zhaoming, upon receiving the report, immediately took with him Coroner Wang Chengyi, Clerk Li Shixian, Bailiff Zhou Yizhu, Zhu Wancheng, and others, and went to the countryside by car for an inquest. The inquest determined that the corpse had indeed committed suicide before death. Since there were no family members, Tu was ordered to prepare a coffin for burial.

Tax Police Officer Commits Suicide by Shooting Himself

Wang Changgui, a police officer of the Fourth Patrol Boat under the jurisdiction of the Third Squadron of the Sixth District of the Fifth Tax Police Corps of Jiangsu Province of the Ministry of Finance, stationed at Ziyang Academy in Huishan Town in this county, was 26 years old and a native of Taixing Coast Town. Because he was fond of prostitutes, he often frequented lower-class brothels and contracted syphilis. Recently, his lymph nodes had become severely inflamed, and his lower body had ulcerated. Medical treatment was ineffective, and he was in extreme pain. He suddenly had thoughts of ending his life. So, at about 12:00 noon yesterday, he took a rifle, loaded it with a bullet, took off the sock on his right foot, used a white cloth strip, tied one end to the big toe, and the other end to the trigger. The muzzle of the gun was aimed at his chest. He stepped on it with his foot, triggering the gun. With a loud bang, the bullet entered from the front of his heart and exited from the right side of his neck. He immediately died, lying in a pool of blood. Later, Li Jinsheng, a police officer on the same boat, learned of the incident and immediately reported it to Squadron Leader Zhang Xintao and sent a letter to the court for an inquest. Prosecutor Shen took the official to the scene and confirmed that the deceased Wang Changgui had indeed committed suicide with a rifle. He ordered the head of the Tu, Jiang Zixian, to prepare a coffin for burial and wait for his family to come to Wuxi to claim the coffin.

Danyang 77

Warehouse Robbed in Lücheng

The warehouse of the Lücheng Farmers' Bank in the eastern countryside of the county was robbed of 20 dan of white rice and 8 dan and 1 dou of wheat by thieves in the late night of the 12th of this month. After the bank discovered the incident, it immediately reported it to the Eighth Police Station and requested arrest and punishment. Upon receiving the report, Inspector He immediately ordered Cui Er, the night watchman of the town, and police officers to search for the suspects. They soon arrested suspect Li Xiaogen, who confessed that the case was committed by boatmen Sha Shouren and Li Changgen from Xinghua. However, their whereabouts are uncertain, but Li Changgen's brother-in-law, Wang Laoer (currently residing in Minghuang Town, Wujin), was arrested, and their residence can be learned from him. Inspector He, according to the confession, dispatched police to Wujin to investigate. Unexpectedly, the suspects' boats were docked in the Beidou River in Wujin. The First Police Station of the Wujin County Public Security Bureau detained them because their whereabouts were suspicious. The police officers of the Eighth Station also arrested a boat of Sha Shouren and learned of the above situation. They returned to the station to report. Inspector He immediately prepared a document to go to Wujin to bring the suspects. However, the Wujin Public Security Bureau refused to allow them to bring the suspects on the grounds that Sha Shouren and others had committed a robbery case in the county. The police officers then escorted Sha Shouren's boat and his wife, Gu, and four children, to Danyang and transferred them to the General Bureau for review.

Malignant Malaria Spreads

Recently, malignant malaria has been spreading in the border area between Tong and Ru, with the most severe infections in Chahe and Shuangdian in Rugao County, no less severe than the plague. Coffins have been sold out. Because there are not enough doctors to allocate, a mobile medical team has been organized to provide treatment.
