Letter to the Editor 128

To the Editor:

I, Cao Guilin, from Tongrentang Chinese Medicine Store, one of the involved parties in the matter, am writing to you directly. I was shocked to read in your newspaper on the 2nd of this month the news that our store was distributing counterfeit Liushen Pills from the Tongchuntang medicine store opened by Zhu Qingxi, and that more than 3,000 boxes of fake pills were confiscated by the French police, and that an apprentice was detained. Although our store did once purchase the Tongchuntang brand of Liushen Pills from Tongchuntang, the packaging and trademarks were all of that store's brand. Our store has been established for many years, so how could we dare to purchase and distribute counterfeit goods? Later, because sales were poor, we switched to purchasing from Lei Yushang, and we still have many pots of stock to this day. As for your newspaper's claim that 3,000 boxes were confiscated and an apprentice was detained, this is absolutely untrue. The fact is that a few days ago, while I, Guilin, was out, several people claiming to be detectives from the Chinese area came to the store and used intimidating language. The shop assistants ignored them because there was no fact of distributing counterfeit Liushen Pills. When I, Guilin, returned to the store, I originally intended to report this to the French police, but because I did not know the names of the people who came, I did not investigate further. The various details published in your newspaper, I believe, were fabricated by a third party, with the intention of undermining our store's business, and were caused by the reporter's mistaken investigation. As this matter concerns our store's reputation and business, and for the sake of your newspaper's accuracy, in addition to taking separate legal action, we request that your lawyer send a letter of correction, etc. Accordingly, we are sending this letter to your newspaper, hoping that you will make the above corrections. Sincerely, to the Editorial Department of the Shen Bao Newspaper Office, Shanghai. Lawyer Sun Zhixiang, October 3rd.

Special Issue for the October 4th World Animal Day Convention

Foreword 130

— Ye Gongchuo

Some say that in these troubled times and in this autumn of changing circumstances, is it not contrary to the times to promote animal protection instead of engaging in practical work? I say it seems so, but it is not. International wars, although they have various political causes, are in fact instigated by a few warmongers. No matter who the instigators are, the result is that victory ultimately belongs to those who have construction and production in the rear, that is my assertion. Animal protection, on the surface, does not directly help our country's current crisis, but it is a crucial part of building people's hearts and minds. In recent times, customs have become debased and morality has declined. The promotion of the Eight Virtues of the New Life Movement is also a jolt to the head, an act of awakening from a dream. Guan Zhong said, "The greatest sorrow is the death of the heart." Even if a country is weakened to the extreme, if the people's hearts do not die, there is always hope. Moreover, war is a momentary change, while construction is the foundation of a country for ten thousand years. Therefore, since the establishment of this association, three years have passed in an instant. Over the years, we have resisted public opinion and adhered to the teachings of the sages, who believed in the unity of all beings and the nurturing of all life. We have diligently carried out advocacy work to revive the decline of people's hearts. Fortunately, we have received sympathy and support from all sides, and the association's work has progressed daily. This year, we are also holding an exhibition of animal protection writings and paintings from schools at all levels in this city, with the aim of deeply imprinting the ancient virtues of benevolence and universal love in the minds of children, so that pure minds can retain good images from an early age. Sun Yat-sen said, "Revolution must first revolutionize the heart." The purpose of animal protection is such, how can it be said to be contrary to the times? The guest said, "Yes, yes." I command it, and write this as the opening remarks of the special issue. However, this matter is of great importance, and my own strength is insufficient. I still rely on the generosity of gentlemen at home and abroad to assist us.

A Brief Account of the Association's Work in the Past Year 131

— Guan Jiong

Time flies like a fleeting shadow. The annual World Animal Day has arrived in an instant. Looking back, this association has been established for more than three years. Its past work was reported in summary in the animal protection days of the previous two years. In the most recent year, thanks to the enthusiastic assistance of people from all walks of life and all members, the association's work has progressed. Although limited by the environment and constrained by finances, all matters concerning animal protection that should be handled have not been fully promoted, the advocacy and publicity work seems to have achieved considerable success. Now, I would like to make a brief report on the association's work in the past year as follows.

(1) Undertakings: Regarding matters of appeal, in addition to appealing to the local governments to ban the killing and eating of plowing cattle and paddy frogs, and to stop the killing of stray dogs and the skinning of unborn lambs, etc., based on the reports of various members and people from all over the country, each case has been handled separately. In April, we also petitioned the Legislative Yuan to enact a law prohibiting animal cruelty. Recently, we jointly drafted a simple charter for banning dog catching and improving treatment with the Shanghai Western Association for the Prevention of Cruelty to Animals, and sent a letter to the Municipal Health Bureau for approval and implementation. At the same time, we also submitted a request to the Ministry of the Interior to issue a national ban on slaughter for one day on Animal Day, October 4th this year. Regarding matters of releasing animals, for those in this city who send animals to the association for release, we will find ways to transfer them to the Dachang Huisheng Society and the Municipal Zoo for raising. The association is currently planning to build a release garden in the near future. We have already obtained the consent of the Wusong Bao'an Temple to lease 35 mu of vacant land permanently. Construction can begin as soon as the funds are raised.

(2) Organization: Our country has a vast territory, and the situations in various places are quite different. If we want to promote animal protection, we are afraid that we will not be able to reach everywhere. Therefore, according to the original plan, we have widely established branches. Currently, there are four established branches in Xijing (Chang'an), Wuxian, Nanjing, and Changsha. There are three branches under preparation in Rugao, Dongtai, and Nanchang. We also began to recruit members on Animal Day last year, in order to gather ideas and jointly plan implementation. In the past year, 286 new members have joined the association. (3) Publicity: In recent times, the trend of human cruelty has become deeply entrenched. Therefore, the association's publicity work must strive to be widespread, in order to arouse the attention of people in society. In the spring, we hired eight promoters to go to various places to investigate. If they encounter any acts of animal cruelty, they will immediately dissuade them with gentle words, and explain the meaning of treating all beings as equals and nurturing all life. In the summer, we reprinted 10,000 animal protection paper fans and distributed them to people in this city, which were warmly welcomed by all sectors and eagerly sought after. They were all distributed in a few days. Recently, we have also produced a kind of animal protection merit badge, which is worn on the lapel. It can arouse our interest in animal protection. It is also the meaning of the ancients wearing strings of beads to warn themselves. On the 3rd and 4th of this month, we will hold an exhibition of animal protection writings and paintings from schools at all levels in this city at the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, so that citizens can have a deep impression and widely promote the meaning of cherishing life.

The above are the major events. There are still many matters to be handled in the future, which need to be carried out step by step. We sincerely hope that kind people at home and abroad will provide guidance and assistance with their strength. I am extremely grateful and offer my prayers.

Loving Creatures 132

— Fan Deyi

"Universal Love" is one of Dr. Sun Yat-sen's principles. The "universal love" he advocated certainly refers to the mutual love and care between human beings. Mencius also said, "Everyone has a heart that cannot bear to see the suffering of others," and also said, "He who has no heart of compassion is not human." The so-called "heart that cannot bear to see the suffering of others" and "heart of compassion" certainly also refer to the emotions that individuals feel from the heart for their own kind. However, we all hope that all animals live lively lives. Who can bear to hear their moans when they are sick and their cries when they are dying? This proves that the heart of compassion is not only for one's own kind. However, some people with abnormal psychology are not fierce to humans, but have狰狞 faces and cruel means to other animals. Take the farmer as an example, he bows and obeys the landlord, shrinking in fear. That pitiful attitude is utterly pitiful. However, when dealing with the cattle that help with the work, he shouts at them every day, making them work all day long, either plowing the fields or scooping water, with no time to rest. Occasionally, because they are too tired from work, they are occasionally lazy, and then they are whipped and beaten. As for their living conditions, there is no need to mention them. The stalls are never cleaned, and the food is never adjusted. How can this not increase their mortality rate and reduce their growth rate?

The same is true for horses. They labor all day long, carrying hundreds of pounds of goods on their bodies, transporting them back and forth. The only reward they get is the master's whip and an unsuitable resting place.

Chickens and ducks are provided for people to eat. Roosters can crow at dawn, and hens can lay eggs. They are also beneficial to humans. However, many people hold them upside down. Try to put yourself in their place and think about how uncomfortable they must be at that time. When it comes time to kill them, some people even pluck the feathers from their necks first before killing them. This is too inconsiderate. Their being killed is already cruel enough, let alone suffering this even more inhumane crime before death.

Dogs and cats are also livestock. We use them to protect us because dogs can guard the door and cats can catch mice. Therefore, they are beneficial animals. Some playful children arbitrarily beat dogs and cats, causing their skin and flesh to suffer. What is the reason for this?

If we want to love and protect them, so that their mortality rate can be reduced, we must often wash their fur, often clean their bedding, and reduce their workload, so that they do not suffer physical pain. This is the true expression of the "heart of compassion" and the original intention of universal love!

One winter, Europe was unusually cold. Many mandarin ducks in Lake Geneva froze to death. The authorities sent medical vehicles to rescue them. I looked down from the building and thought of the hundreds of millions of refugees in my homeland, wandering in the wind and snow, not worth a glance from the wealthy and noble. Living in a foreign land, I felt that some people were inferior to things. I wrote three poems and sent them to the Animal Protection Association.

Middle-aged sorrow and joy oppress the rest of my life.

From now on, I am afraid to spend another snowy sea.

Embroidered quilts are idly piled up like Yue Ejun's.

May the heavenly flowers scatter spring cotton seeds.

Why must we pity only the ornamental birds?

The ethereal soul does not scatter with the clouds and smoke.

A new sorrow in my journey, an epitaph for a crane.

I remember combing my wings in the wind of falling plum blossoms.

Who will share the desolate countryside in the wind and snow?

Warmth protects all living beings, creating a brocade cloud.

May we all cross over together, vowing to be boundless.

Waiting to realize the promise of our hearts for a hundred thousand years.

Draft from Bicheng

Family Animal Protection Song 133

— Hu Bing

Don't hold ducks and chickens upside down.

Try to compare it to yourself.

Keeping dogs requires cleanliness.

Dirtiness is annoying.

Paddy frogs protect grain insects.

My heart aches when I eat them.

Cattle and sheep provide many benefits.

Don't whip them lightly.

The little sparrows under the eaves.

The homeowner must love them.

Holding them upside down is bitterly miserable.

Hanging them up is the same taste.

Don't make them dirty.

The sight of it is also embarrassing.

Don't buy them to eat.

How can you bear to eat beneficial insects?

Raising them requires cherishing them.

Prevent them from shedding tears.

Chirping expresses happiness.

Carefully warn children not to catch them.

Psychological Construction for Animal Protection 134

— Yang Mou

Animal protection in China is still a nascent movement. Protecting life is human nature, but this nature is gradually being extinguished. Sun Yat-sen said, "Revolution must first revolutionize the heart." The foundation of animal protection is to revolutionize the heart. In everyone's mind, building a solid line of defense for animal protection will ensure that the effectiveness of animal protection can be counted on.

So how can we build this psychological defense line for animal protection? In my opinion, it can be divided into four points:

(1) Everyone must have a spirit of universal love

Humans are originally full of universal love, and they have a passion for protecting all living things. The decline of this spirit of universal love and the increasing cruelty of killing creatures, the first reason is the mischief of human selfishness.

Selfish psychology is a manifestation of human inferiority. For the sake of personal interests, they do not hesitate to make any sacrifices, and innocent animals encounter tragic fates.

I once saw a person buy a new handgun and use stray dogs as targets. When that poor dog lay inexplicably in a pool of blood, stretching its legs in the final struggle of life, that person showed a proud and狰狞 smile. I have also met a gentleman who likes to raise birds. He does not hesitate to use thousands of small green insects as food for his birds. There was also a parent who was frightened by a frog and, after encountering frogs, beat them to death alive! ... Ah! These and those, it is truly endless. These are full of selfish psychology performances, truly a great shame and insult to mankind;

To overcome these selfish psychologies, everyone must have a spirit of universal love. What is the spirit of universal love? It is a rich sense of sympathy. We must love ourselves, and we must love others. We must love people, and we must love things. We must sacrifice the interests of the small self to maintain the interests of hundreds of thousands of lives.

(2) Everyone must have a spirit of diligence

The second obstacle to be broken psychologically in the animal protection movement is the psychology of pleasure. "Enjoying the present" is a traditional concept. Countless animals have sacrificed their lives under the psychology of people enjoying the present.

Not to mention wealthy families, even "peddlers and hawkers" and "those who sell soup from carts" have a few dollars in hand today, they have to buy half a catty of meat and a fish, kill a chicken, make soup with wine, and drink and eat at home. When they are in a good mood, they may even add a few Yangcheng Lake red crabs. The people eating are eating with joy, but how can they know the moans of pigs, the struggles of fish, the cries of chickens, and the tragic scene of crabs being trapped in a hot pot?

To overcome this psychology of pleasure, everyone must have a spirit of diligence. Vegetables are indeed not as delicious as fish and meat, cotton batting is indeed not as warm as fox fur, and tofu is indeed not as nourishing as young chicken juice… But for the sake of the life of a member of the biological world, we would rather give up this and choose that. This kind of material diligence is rewarding, and that is the great spiritual pleasure!

(3) Everyone must have a pragmatic spirit

"Wine pools and meat forests" are symbols of family extravagance. Without delicacies from land and sea on the banquet table, it cannot be considered a formal wine banquet. Families with weddings and happy events often boast of how many pigs and sheep they have slaughtered and how many chickens and ducks they have killed to show off the greatness of their "排场". People who do not wear fox-lined or squirrel-skin coats in winter cannot be considered well-off. Misses and madams who do not have a fox fur collar cannot be considered nobles. If this social psychology of competing for vanity is not eradicated, those innocent lives will be slaughtered in batches by cruel humans;

To eradicate this psychology of vanity, everyone must have a sincere heart to create blessings for animals! Everyone should change their past attitude. Using the means of killing animals to show our luxury is shameful, cruel, and barbaric. It is a manifestation of the primitive beastliness of human beings and cannot be tolerated in modern civilized society.

(4) Everyone must have the spirit of courage

Some people say, "I really want to practice animal protection, but my strength is small, and it has no effect, and sometimes I am laughed at." This kind of excuse of "everyone does this, so I do this" is a manifestation of utter laziness and a manifestation of the psychology of fearing difficulties and seeking peace of mind. To achieve success in animal protection, this psychology must also be removed.

First, we must "start with me, regardless of whether others do it or not."

Sports News

Our World Games Delegation Arrives in Shanghai: A Total of Eighty-Five Male and Female Team Members Arrive; Attend a Welcome Tea Party Held by Various Organizations in the Afternoon 135

Our country's delegation to the World Games and the delegation for sports youth inspection in Germany, led by head Wang Zhengting, arrived in Shanghai at 1:00 PM yesterday aboard the Italian mail ship Conte Rosso. The Shanghai Physical Education Association arranged the Suilin Apartment as the delegation's accommodation. At 4:00 PM that afternoon, various organizations in the city held a joint welcome meeting at the YMCA. The details are as follows:

Port Arrangement: The ship docked at the China Merchants Bureau North Wharf. A portion of the welcoming representatives traveled by the scheduled City Ferry No. 5 from the New Customs Wharf at 12:15 PM to welcome them, while another group stood waiting at the wharf. The Aviation Association specially dispatched the Save-the-Nation No. 1 and No. 2 aircraft to welcome them at the Wusong Estuary. The gate of the China Merchants Bureau North Wharf was adorned with crossed Party and national flags, and a banner reading "All Circles of Shanghai Welcome the Return of the World Games Delegation" was hung high. A colorful archway was erected on the wharf. All welcoming personnel were equipped with welcome flags, creating a lively atmosphere.

Welcome from All Sectors: The Shanghai Public Security Bureau and the Songhu Garrison Headquarters each dispatched a band to play music at the port. City Ferry No. 5 met the Conte Rosso near the Fish Market. As the ship docked, the welcoming personnel boarded to greet the delegation, including Wu Shizhang's representative Li Dachao, Director Zhou Jue of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs Shanghai Office, Public Security Bureau Chief Cai Jingjun, Secretary Wang Zhinan of the Garrison Headquarters, Jianghai Customs Superintendent Zhu Changnian, Legislator Li Denghui, General Secretary Shen Ciliang of the National Sports Advancement Association, Jian Shiqin of the Shanghai Debt Bureau, as well as representatives from the Municipal Stadium, the Chinese Physical Education Association, the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, the Chinese Boy Scout Council, Mao Heyuan from the Ningbo Association, the Jingwu Athletic Association, the Aviation Association, the YMCA, the Southeast Women's Physical Education College, Liangjiang Normal School, China Women's Physical Education School, and the private Zhong, Guoguang Middle School, Chengzhong Middle School, Dongya Physical Education College, Jushenghe Athletic Association, Qinfen Bookstore, Xiayi Society, Zhiguang Society, etc.

Landing and Departure for Accommodation: After a brief exchange of greetings with the welcoming personnel, the delegation lined up neatly on the wharf and shouted "Long live China" three times. They then boarded the city ferry to the New Customs Wharf and disembarked, setting off firecrackers as they left. They proceeded to the Zheng Apartment in Germany for rest. Head Wang Zhengting returned directly to his residence from the China Merchants Bureau North Wharf.

Welcome Tea Party: At 4:00 PM, various organizations in the city held a tea party at the YMCA on Eight Immortals Bridge to welcome the delegation. Attendees included the delegation, the inspection team, Wu Mayor's representative Li Dachao, Liu Xuefang of the Municipal Council, Lu Shuang, Wu Kaisheng of the National Road Association, Jia Siwu of the Public Security Bureau, Xu Zhiyi of the Chinese Physical Education Association, Luo Beichen of the China Insurance Company, He Dekui of the Local Association, Li Longbiao of the Jingwu Athletic Association, Zhu Shaoping of the World Chinese Student Association, Zhang Yuliang of the Aviation Association, Zhao Weizu of the Boy Scout Council, Zhang Binghui of the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, Jin Runxiang of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, Jiang Jianbai of the Cultural Construction Association, Zhou Xuexiang of the General Labor Union, Fan Wei of the Garrison Headquarters, Huang Zaoxiong of the Municipal Education Association, Tong Muge of the Municipal Party Headquarters, and Ling Xitao of the YMCA, totaling two hundred people.

Chairman's Speech: Li Dachao, representing Mayor Wu, presided over the meeting and delivered a brief welcoming speech. He Dekui then delivered a welcome speech, stating that it was a great pleasure to meet with everyone after several months apart. He said that the whole country was very concerned about their trip abroad. Although the results were lagging behind, failure is the mother of success, and he hoped that they would continue to work hard. He said that their trip to Europe to compete in sports with advanced European and American countries, even in defeat, was honorable. He believed that if the world held competitions in other fields (such as commerce and industry), the results of our country would be even worse than those shown by participating in the World Games. He hoped that they would not belittle themselves but invigorate their spirits and strive for the future.

Jiang Jianbai's Speech: Jiang Jianbai then delivered a speech, stating that competition always has victories and defeats. If strength is not as good as others, one must conserve energy and wait for the future. Hearing is not as good as seeing, and seeing is not as good as being there in person. He believed that they had gained a lot of practical experience from this trip and that if they could continue to work hard based on what they had learned from observation, their future success could be anticipated. Two students from Liangjiang Women's School then presented flowers, which were accepted by Wang Zhengting on behalf of the delegation.

Wang Zhengting's Speech: Wang Zhengting, the head of the delegation, replied, stating that he was both grateful and ashamed for the warm welcome and reception given to the Chinese World Games delegation upon their return. He said that sports are a matter for the entire country and cannot be represented by a few athletes. It is of great importance to national rejuvenation and the physical strength of the people. He said that he deeply felt from this trip that sports are widespread and developed in various countries, and their results are naturally good. Moreover, sports can stimulate national concepts and are an important strategy for establishing a country. He said that he knew that this trip would be a failure, but in order to seek improvement, it was necessary to have a clear understanding of the advantages of advanced countries and the shortcomings of oneself. The purpose of the delegation was precisely this. Although the results were not as good as others, they strived to compete, hoping that others would have some understanding of our country's sports spirit. The government and the people should jointly identify the direction and fundamentally improve. Therefore, there was also an organization for the inspection team. He said that the only result of this trip was to give people in various countries considerable attention. The sixty-nine athletes, including track and field, ball games, and marathon events, had made much progress compared to their participation in Los Angeles. Among them, the Chinese martial arts performance along the way had won much praise. In the future, he hoped that the whole country would unanimously promote sports, strive for training, and pay attention to methods to increase the physical strength of the people. In the future, the board of directors of the National Sports Advancement Association will discuss the reports of the delegation and the inspection team, so as to seek improvement, report to the government, and make public announcements for all sectors to adopt and implement. He said that since they are about to disperse, he hoped that they would not be discouraged by failure but would work harder because of failure. He also intended to petition the government to promote sports more effectively in the future, because sports are the basic work of education.

Issuing Certificates: After the speech, World Games certificates were issued, along with certificates for the delegation and the inspection team. The original text was: "The Eleventh World Games will be held in Berlin, Germany, from August 1st to 16th, 1936. Mr./Ms. so-and-so is selected as a member of the so-and-so team of the Chinese delegation. This certificate is hereby issued." It was signed by the Chairman of the Chinese National Sports Advancement Association and the Head of the Chinese World Games Delegation, Wang Zhengting, and the General Secretary, Shen Siliang. Finally, Wang Shifu, who had just returned from Turkey, delivered a speech. The meeting adjourned around 5:00 PM.

National Arts Honor: According to the National Arts Team, after the closing ceremony, the team performed in Foshan, Frankfurt, Wiesbaden, Star, and other places, and was very welcomed, indicating that the Germans were very interested in Chinese martial arts. It is said that the team has reported everything to Chu Minyi by letter.

Return Itinerary: The delegation left Berlin on the 1st, arrived in Rome on the 2nd, and boarded the ship in Naples on the 4th, setting sail at 1:00 PM in the afternoon. The journey was smooth and calm. More than 40 Japanese athletes also traveled on the same ship. When in Bombay, it was planned to hold a triangular track and field competition between China, Japan, and India, but it did not materialize. When the ship passed Singapore, it encountered wind and waves, and most of the members of our delegation were seasick. In addition, Feng Youzhen, a special correspondent from the Central News Agency, is still staying in Europe for inspection.

Departures for Home: After the banquet held by various organizations yesterday, the Shanxi Sports Association distributed travel expenses, and the delegation and inspection team were free to act. It is said that many people left Shanghai last night, and the rest will leave Shanghai in the next couple of days. In addition, the Chinese Physical Education Association is scheduled to host the delegation at the YMCA at 2:00 PM this afternoon.

List of Team Members Arriving in Shanghai: The list of members of the delegation and the inspection team who arrived in Shanghai yesterday aboard the Conte Rosso is as follows: Wang Zhengting, Hao Gengsheng, Zhou Jiaqi, Shi Zhaokang, Yu Hengzhi, Shu Hong, Lu Xiangqian, Zou Bingquan, Chen Zhenhe, Sun Jinshun, Jia Youliang, Wang Yuzeng, Wang Nanzhen, Mou Zuoyun, Wang Hongbin, Li Shaotang, Liu Yunzhang, Shen Yugong, Liu Baocheng, Feng Nianhua, Wang Shixuan, Yin Guiren, Yu Jingxiao, Xu Zhaoxiong, Song Junfu, Shen Kunnan, Chen Baoqiu, Wang Shilin, Huang Yingjie, Liu Changchun, Dai Shuguo, Fu Baolu, Zhou Changxing, Zhang Jiakui, Hao Chunde, Li Sen, Cai Zhengyi, Zhou Yuyu, Zhang Zaojiu, Zheng Chengshan, Ye Liang, Shen Liang, Weng Kangting, Li Menghua, Wang Runlan, Xi Guidi, Zhan Gui, Gu Shunhua, Zhang Wenguang, Wen Jingming, Zheng Huaixian, Jin Shisheng, Zhang Erding, Kou Yunliu, Zhai Lianyuan, Chuan Shuyun, Liu Yuhua, Yuan Dunli, Wu , Gao Zi, Zhao Wenzao, Hu Anshan, Wu Bangwei, Li Zhou, Shao Rugan, Chuan Jingru, Hou Luoxun, Qian Yiqin, Jin Zhaojun, Peng Wenyu, Xia Xiang, Wang Huaiqi, Jiang Zhensui, Wang Shoufang, Chen , De, Du Yufei, Chen Yongsheng, Huang Liming, Du Longyuan, Zhang Huilan, Xie Wenqiu, etc., a total of eighty-five people.

Mr. Wang Zhengting, Head of Delegation, and Others Talk About Their Impressions of Participating in the World Games 138

Dr. Wang Zhengting, the head of the delegation, talked about his impressions of participating in the World Games as follows: (1) The results of our country's delegation to the World Games were known before going abroad. The reason for participating was to gain experience. This was the first official participation, as only one person participated in the previous Los Angeles World Games. It is deeply hoped that participation will attract the attention of the entire nation. Although the results of the National Games and several Far Eastern Games have been reported in the newspapers, they have not received sufficient attention from the people. This participation in the World Games, in comparison, will make the people aware of the disparity in strength and strive to improve. (2) The cause of sports requires the attention of the general public, but it also requires the government to vigorously promote it in order to be widespread and deep-rooted. Sports are the foundation of education. Only with a healthy body can there be a healthy spirit. For thousands of years, our country has emphasized literature and belittled martial arts, and this habit has been ingrained for a long time. The biggest reason for the failure of this participation in the World Games is insufficient physical strength. It is hoped that the government's education authorities will pay attention to this. The physical fitness of the people and the future of the nation are deeply dependent. (3) In sports competitions, physical strength is one thing, and technique is another. Our country's physical strength is indeed insufficient, and the technique is not satisfactory. Therefore, it is very important to conduct technical research in a scientific way. In addition to selecting athletes, there is also an organization for the sports inspection team. The members of each team are all sports directors of various universities and sports researchers, hoping to contribute what they have learned to the government and the people, as a basis for future reform and innovation. (4) The next World Games will be held in Tokyo in four years, which is very close to our country. At that time, athletes from various countries will definitely come to China for sightseeing after participating in the conference. It is deeply hoped that our country's government and people will prepare in advance so as to give a good impression to people from all groups. (5) I have been promoting sports for more than thirty years, but I have not yet been able to develop a sports talent, which is very regrettable, etc. It is reported that Mr. Wang will stay in Shanghai for a day or two, go to Beijing to pay respects to the authorities and report on the progress, and then go to the United States to take up a new post.

Hao Gengsheng Talks About the Inspection Team Leader Hao Gengsheng Talks About His Impressions of Sports in Various Countries, Saying: (1) From this inspection of various countries, I feel that there are many strengths of other countries, and very few of them are truly unknown to the Chinese people. What is regrettable is that people have specific and practical plans and implement them step by step, while we know but do not act, which is the same as not knowing. The reason for this is the problem of people. For example, during the World Games, Germany convened sports researchers from various countries to organize an international student sports camp. The head of the camp was free to move around, but he stayed in the camp during the World Games and never left, never visiting the World Games for a single day. This kind of dedication to duty and willingness to take responsibility is worthy of emulation. If the Chinese people can have the same spirit and the same concept, then there is nothing in the world that cannot be done. (2) Although the government has been vigorously promoting sports in our country in recent years, it has attracted general attention, but the degree of attention is still not as high as the general level in various countries, and we must continue to intensify our efforts, not only in terms of verbal theory but also fully expressed in actual action. (3) Considering the trend of education in various countries, I feel that the position of education in our country in the future must take the physical fitness of the people as the priority of all education. The first principle of education is to exercise the body. Sports are the foundation of morality and intelligence. Only with a strong body can we cultivate morality and study and become an ideal and healthy citizen. (4) Considering the progress of various countries, it is due to their ability to take the strengths of others and make up for their own shortcomings, and to have the courage to reform. If our country wants to make progress in sports, it can only do so by striving to implement them. Although each country has its own national conditions, and what is applicable to other countries may not be entirely suitable for China, it is also necessary to abandon the short and adopt the long, and take the essence and use it extensively, etc.

Shao Rugan Talks

(1) The results of this World Games have made significant progress compared with the past. Although our delegation has no performance to comfort the people of the country, the participants have done their best. Due to the disparity in physique and the slightly poor skills, the results are relatively poor. However, the participation of a large number of people has attracted the attention of hundreds of thousands of spectators, which is enough to change international hearing. (2) The precious records of the World Games are not accidental. They have considerable strength and superb skills. This level cannot be achieved without persistent practice. (3) Only when the people have a general interest in sports can outstanding talents be produced, and the enthusiastic promotion of the government and the people is necessary. (4) Each movement has a unique consciousness to promote. In the future, the sports community in our country should also pay close attention to this, and it is most important to popularize the concept of national sports. (5) Examining sports in various European countries, their unique consciousness is formed by the background of their society, country, and politics. The administrative group of sports has been based on political organization. Without government control, there will be no effect of promotion and development. (6) The inspection team has completed the first draft of the report, with detailed suggestions on sports in our country in the future. Adopting the strengths of others, making up for our own shortcomings, and working hard, we may be able to raise our heads in Tokyo in 1940, etc.

Jin Zhaojun Talks

Politicians and educators in various countries regard sports as a basic cause for strengthening the nation and establishing the country. In this World Games, in addition to sports competitions, there are also gatherings on sports education issues, which can prove that the above-mentioned statement is not wrong. The environments of various countries are different, so European and American countries mostly create a sports national policy that adapts to the special environment based on their own national environment. This phenomenon is particularly evident in Britain, the United States, Germany, Italy, Denmark, and Sweden. The above-mentioned countries all have special and significant sports effects. Therefore, my first impression is that the sports national policy of the Republic of China must also be based on our special environment and determine a plan of at least ten years of training in order to revive the Chinese nation. The second impression is that the average development of sports in various countries is not as distorted as in our country. They have integrated society and schools. In our country, social sports are far inferior to others. Even when it comes to school sports, the problem of elementary school sports has not yet been studied and practically done by anyone. Even middle and high schools at all levels also present a phenomenon of divergent development. This is the second urgent matter to be resolved. The last impression is that the authorities in European and American countries mostly have the spirit of burying themselves in work. This is a kind of spirit that we currently need most.

Cai Wenli Talks About the Failure of Football and Basketball 139

When Cai Wenli landed in Singapore, he talked with Xue Guangqian, the president of Shanghai News Agency, who returned on the same ship. European football tactics and methods are peculiar. The center half only stays in a straight line in front and behind. The two full-backs and the left and right center half-backs are one in front and one behind. Sometimes the full-back intrudes to the left and right flanks of the striker and also defends the position of the full-back. The ball is passed as smoothly as we play basketball, and it is foolproof. The ball thrown out of bounds at the goal can be thrown to the opponent's goal, just like a normal corner kick. Watching professional football games in the UK is amazing. Observing its training methods is convincing. After our team was eliminated by the UK, they left Berlin on August 11th and went to various countries to observe. There were a total of seven exhibition games, one win, one draw, and five losses. The performance in the game in Paris was the best. People in various European countries were very impressed with the sportsmanship of our team. Regarding the criticism on the technology, it is so-called "clean," so the impression of our team is very deep. As for the reasons for the failure, there are three points: (1) Insufficient physical strength; (2) Inaccurate passing; The weather conditions. As for the previous Hong Kong report that Li Guowei died due to injury, it is completely unfounded. Also, in the friendly basketball games in Germany, they won against Italy and Peru, and lost to the United States. In the official game, they first met Japan and unfortunately lost. They then won against France, and finally lost to Peru and Brazil. Looking at the reasons for the failure in the game against Japan, (1) the players were flustered on the court and could not fully display their skills; (2) the tactics were stagnant and they could not adapt to changes, and they were arbitrarily arranged by the enemy and could not cope with it. In the penalty kicks alone, our country had fifteen opportunities to throw the ball into the basket, but only two goals were scored, which is a pity.

The Situation of the Inspection Team Will Be Grouped for Research and Compilation of Reports 140

A total of thirty-seven male and female members of the sports inspection team to Germany, except for Li Youling and Xu Yingchao, who went to Springfield University in the United States to specialize in sports, Wu Demao, Le Xianqu, Huang Yunzhi (female) who stayed in Germany for inspection and research on sports, Cui Yalan who went to the United States to study sports, and Xu Minhui who went to the United Kingdom, France, Russia and other countries for inspection and planned to return to China via Siberia next month, the remaining thirty members, led by head Hao Gengsheng, returned to China. Among them, Ye Guantang, Liu Quanduo, Guo Songtang, and Tan Yingbin had already landed in Xianghuai, and a total of twenty-six members arrived in Shanghai.

Inspection Process: The inspection team traveled to seven countries, a total of nine places, namely Berlin and Dresden in Germany, Stockholm in Sweden, Copenhagen in Denmark, Prague in the Czech Republic, Vienna in Austria, Budapest in Hungary, and Rome in Italy. Among the countries, the longest time was spent in Germany, living in an international school camp. The observers were mostly sports specialty schools, as well as elementary schools. In Dresden, they visited elementary and secondary school sports and the world-famous Art Student Museum. The other six countries traveled for a total of seventeen days. The shortest time was spent in the Czech Republic, only half a day, and the longest time was spent in Italy, three days. In Sweden, they visited the Lin's Sports School, which invented Swedish gymnastics. In the Czech Republic, they visited the Sokol Sports Association. In Austria, they visited a girls' middle school. The completeness of the equipment was unmatched by other European countries. There was a special ski course, with four weeks in winter dedicated to skiing. Failure in this course meant that one could not graduate. The school's sports field had no such facilities except for the University of Vienna. Therefore, the government divided the entire city into five districts, each with a sports field for the use of school sports in the district. The method was economical and could be adopted. In Hungary, they visited a sports specialty school. The school produced a large number of talents. Most of the athletes who attended this World Games came from this school. They also visited a sports ground run by the government, with hot spring baths and various sports facilities, which was a good place for public sports. In Italy, they visited a male sports school, the Mussolini Sports Field, and the "Balilla" camp. Overall, the most developed public sports were in Hungary and the Czech Republic, and the most impressive were the two countries of Austria and Italy. The method of compulsory labor for young people in Germany was practical and was a good system in modern times. Italy's "Balilla" youth training, the combination of intelligence, morality, and physical education, and its down-to-earth and pragmatic spirit was unmatched by other countries. When visiting the camp, the ears were filled with music, shooting commands, and the sound of footsteps, which was tragic and majestic, and made people excited. The memories are still lingering today.

Group Research: For the convenience of reporting, the inspection team divided the inspection of sports in various countries into groups for research. On the ship, each team member began to draft the initial report and held a meeting in Singapore to discuss the matter. It is reported that the detailed general report will be compiled into a book by each group and published. The members are divided into groups as follows: Sweden Shao Rugan (convener) Xia Xiang, Jiang Zhensui, Chen Yongsheng, Czech Qian Yiqin (convener) Chuan Jingru, Lu Xiangqian, Du Yufei, Denmark Huang Yanming (convener) Peng Wenyu, Hu Anshan, Ye Guanhe, Germany Zhang Huilan (convener) Wang Shoufang, Yu Yongzuo Guo Songtang, Tan Yingbin, Hungary Wu Bangwei (convener) Shu Hong, Chen Tude, Gao Zi, Italy Jin Zhaojun (convener) Li Zhou, Zhao Wenzao, Du Longyuan, Austria Wang Huaiqi. Shandong Wuhe wheat opened at 5.33 yuan, Ruiwan wheat at 5.3 yuan, Daqiao wheat at 5 yuan, Bengbu wheat at 5.24 yuan, Mingguang wheat at 5.27 yuan. Shen Da bought 8,000 bags.

West New Early Rice Has Been Launched - Trade Still Firm 158

(South Shanghai) Yesterday, the source of each gang was less than before, with a total of nearly 20 goods arriving, totaling 4,000 stone. Chang Gang's West New Early Rice has been launched, the rice quality is round, plump, and is indeed a good product, with a price opening at 10.07 yuan. The market situation of Bailiger Yao was that the opening price rose step by step due to the arrival of scarce and active sales. If Qingdao, Dalian, Longkou and other gang bought more than 400 bags, the result was that the market increased by 0.5 yuan. The new early rice market was the same, and the various new top-quality such as Duyang also followed up 0.3 yuan. However, judging from the phenomenon of the afternoon market, it seemed to have turned weak. This is because after the soaring prices for several consecutive days, there will eventually be a decline. As for the broken hull and thick rice, the price is slightly higher by 0.1 yuan. The thin rice was bought by the gang, with more than 400 bags bought, and the market improved by 0.2 to 0.3 yuan. Chenbian Yuan lacks goods and has no market, and the new Yin Yuan, on the contrary, has an oversupply and a unique drop of 0.1 to 0.2 yuan.

(North Shanghai) Yesterday, the source of each gang in Hexia was more than 120 numbers. The sales of various colors in the market were slightly less than before. The opening price in the morning was due to the residual power of the previous market, so each listed goods was raised and sold out. Broken rice continued to be tight at 0.3 yuan, the price of high-quality new early rice was increased by 0.1 to 0.2 yuan. Zhongjue suddenly rose by 0.3 to 0.4 yuan, and Zhong also increased by 0.2 yuan. Chenxin Sheep Sharp was also expensive at 0.2 to 0.3 yuan, so was the new Du Sharp. The Wharf Tip continued to add 0.1 yuan. Chenbian Yuan was stable, but the various colors turned stable in the evening market.

Ke Xian Sales More Lively 159

Yesterday, the digestion of Ke Xian suddenly became strong, but the arrival was scarce, and the market immediately skyrocketed. The arrival in the past two days was only thousands of bags, but yesterday the number of Japanese customers actually reached more than 20,000 bags, and there was purchasing from Tianjin and other northern gangs, and the situation was more lively. The route to Guangdong and Shantou was endless. In addition to the continuous procurement of the street, inland gangs also embellished, and the cargo owner was no longer as eager to sell as before. The price immediately rose 0.1 to 0.2 yuan. A total of more than 7,000 bags of Jiangxi rice, 8,000 bags of Xiang rice, 4,235 bags of Han rice, and 400 to 5,000 bags of Taiwan, Guangdong and other machine rice were sold throughout the day. Most of the brown rice was bought by the Guangdong gang, while the machine rice was by the Northern and Shantou.

Yellow Soybean Market Strong 160

The recent yellow soybean market has been quite stable, because there are not many goods coming and going, because the new goods are on the market, and only a small number are on the market, so the price of soybean oil in the market is strong, and the market has a good situation. Yesterday, the oil mills, foreign gangs, and the market bought more than 7,000 bags of new beans from each road.

Sesame, Foreign Merchants Buy Continuously 161

The sesame market situation, the spot and futures go in opposite directions, the foreign merchants' term cargo transaction is still deserted, and it is temporarily less optimistic. The spot cargo is briskly sold by the Dongyang gang and the Nanyang Chengbenjie, so although the transaction is only 500 bags, the market is quite stable.

Piece Goods, Printed Cloth Sales Increase Daily, Fabric May Not Be Able to Keep Up, Japanese Factories Sell Out of December Futures, Chinese Factories Plan to Add Printing and Dyeing Finishing Departments 162

Yesterday's cloth market, the situation in this city has indeed turned mild, and the stable market is back to normal, but the standard yarn and flower are both weak, and the current yarn has fallen rapidly. The current cotton cloth price is very profitable based on the current flower price, but the brisk sales of goods is to be feared due to the lack of stock. The booking of the source of goods has been ordered one after another, and the weaving factory has ordered the most fabric, because the sales of printed and finished goods have increased daily in recent years, and printing and dyeing finishing factories have also emerged, and their business is very developed, resulting in a particularly strong demand for fabric, fearing that it may not be able to keep up, and the weaving factory's raw material is mostly East fine line, and it is extremely difficult to obtain current goods. The situation is now best in the Japanese factory, and the December futures have also been sold out. The fabric woven by the factory is also becoming increasingly popular, and the profit of fabric is sold at a far distance compared to fine and coarse cloths. There are also gradual attempts by Chinese textile factories to add printing, dyeing and finishing departments. It is heard that Minfeng, Jiashuang, and Dacheng are about to mature in three or four factories.

Metals　White Lead Sheets Sold Out Upon Arrival 163

White lead sheets are selling very well, and the arrivals are scarce. There are many buyers in the market, but very few sellers. Therefore, the market is quite brisk and poised to rise sharply. The prices for No. 2 grade are 152-153 yuan per barrel; Nos. 3 and 4, 134-135 yuan; No. 5, 128 yuan; Nos. 6 and 7, 124-125 yuan; No. 8, 127-128 yuan; Nos. 9 and 10, around 125 yuan, all up by 2-3 yuan compared to the previous market. The autumn sales of this product are very extensive, but due to the high prices last year, dealers purchased very little, resulting in a current scarcity of imports, and buyers have no stock. As a result, any newly arrived goods are quickly sold out. It was reported yesterday that Gong He Xiang and Xin Tai Gu’s warehouses received over 600 barrels, which were said to have been sold out. Battery factories and agents from other regions were the largest buyers.

Shen Bao Children's Special

Silk and Tea: Silk Merchants Hesitant and Uncertain 164

Yesterday, international silk markets in New York and Yokohama showed mixed fluctuations. Ultimately, sluggish actual sales led to only slight changes. Yokohama spot prices fell by three yuan, while futures fell by one yuan. New York spot prices rose by one and a half points, while forward contracts fell by half a point. Japanese silk 75 and 83 evenness, as well as Shanghai silk 78 evenness, each fell by one point. East silk remained at its original price. In Lyon, financial instability and the devaluation of the French franc are expected to significantly impact French import trade. Consequently, sales of Chinese silk in France may also be somewhat affected. In the local silk market, unpredictable circumstances have created a hesitant and uncertain atmosphere, leading to a significant reduction in silk transactions. It is said that only 72 bales of both domestic and foreign silk were sold yesterday.

Green Tea Sales Show No Improvement 165

Yesterday, the green tea market remained sluggish. European merchants, in response to the French franc devaluation, reduced prices for Moroccan orders by 20%. This made it difficult to proceed with transactions. Only Concord, Tongfu, and other firms purchased a total of over 200 boxes of needle, eyebrow, and pearl tea. Market prices trended downwards. According to a report from the tea warehouse trade association, the green tea market this week was particularly bleak. The reasons cited were the impact of the French franc devaluation, widespread rumors causing anxiety, low tea inventories, and a scarcity of high-quality tea. Foreign firms showed little interest in purchasing. The total sales for the week included 700 boxes of high-quality eyebrow tea, 300 boxes of small needle eyebrow tea, and several hundred boxes of Ping-Shui high-quality eyebrow tea. The market situation is likely to stall for some time.

North-South Goods: Second Batch of New Quanzhou Dried Longan Arrives in Shanghai – Walnut Sales Active…Market Sentiment Tight 166

Large Dried Longan: Due to better development this year, the second batch of Quanzhou large dried longan, consisting of over 6,000 boxes, only arrived in Shanghai on the Yongsheng ship the day before yesterday. It is believed that the quantity is excessive, causing market fatigue. Sales have not yet begun. According to sources, the cost of this batch is high, preventing price reductions. It is likely to be released in stages to avoid market saturation.

Walnuts: Recently, due to active sales, the market sentiment has been quite good. Yesterday, Zhenbang firms sold over 330 packages of Jinan walnuts at 22 yuan. All firms accepted their allocated share, indicating a continued tightening of the market.

Sugar Market: Under-the-Table Trading of Miscellaneous Green Sugar Looks Promising 167

Yesterday, the sugar market continued to tighten slightly. The trade association set the price for #24 coarse granulated sugar at 21.8 yuan for spot goods, up five cents. Re-exported goods were priced at 6.4 yuan. #8 East White sugar was priced at 21.4 yuan for spot goods, up one cent. #9 re-exported YRO mark was priced at 6 yuan, up one cent. Other prices remained unchanged. Cotton white sugar from local factories was priced at the original level. Chaozhou sugar firms only offered 42 packages of Cai Ji red sugar at 14.95 yuan and 49 packages of Fuquan red sugar at 15.65 yuan. Under-the-table trading of 100 packages of miscellaneous green sugar was reported, with the goods being of exceptional quality and priced one to two cents higher.

Spirit, Industry 168

— Mu Jie

Spirit and industry have a close and inseparable relationship.

What is spirit? In broad terms, spirit can be divided into two types: one is the spirit of fearlessness, and the other is the spirit of diligent and enduring perseverance. The combination of these two types of spirit generates the "power" we need to undertake any endeavor. Let me provide a few examples: Consider individuals like the great inventor Thomas Edison and the great scientist Benjamin Franklin. Weren't their successes due to the power of their struggle? Consider groups of people like the French Revolution and the American Revolution. Weren't their successes also due to the power of their struggle? And this struggle is rooted in the two types of spirit mentioned above. Let's take Dr. Sun Yat-sen's revolution as an example. If Dr. Sun Yat-sen did not possess these two types of spirit, how could he have brought about the Xinhai Revolution? He would have succumbed to the numerous failures he faced along the way!

"Power" is the driving force behind successful endeavors. And only spirit can generate "power." Therefore, spirit and industry have a close and inseparable relationship.

Children, remember this! Spirit is unique to humankind. One unit of spirit yields one unit of industry.

Random Chats on Children's Anecdotes 169

— Yi Sheng

Emperor Ming Debates the Sun

When Emperor Ming of the Jin Dynasty was only a few years old, he was sitting on his father, Emperor Yuan's, lap one day. Someone arrived from Chang'an, reporting news from Luoyang. Emperor Yuan shed tears silently. Emperor Ming asked, "Why are you crying?" Emperor Yuan explained his intention to cross the river eastward in detail and casually asked him, "Do you think Chang'an is farther away, or the sun, my child?" He replied, "The sun is far away because we have never heard of anyone coming from the sun." Emperor Yuan was delighted to see that he had such insight at such a young age. The next day, Emperor Yuan held a gathering of officials and mentioned that conversation. He asked Emperor Ming the same question again in front of everyone. Unexpectedly, today, he replied that "the sun is near." Emperor Yuan's expression changed, likely because he wanted to show off his son's intelligence but ended up making a mess of things. He asked sternly, "Why is your answer different today from yesterday?" Emperor Ming slowly explained, "Upon closer reflection, we see the sun when we raise our eyes, but we cannot see Chang'an."

"How far away is the sun from us? How long a bamboo pole would it take to reach the sun?..." These questions have probably swirled in the young minds of many children. Sadly, even after consulting with adults, they remain unsatisfied! In fact, adults should seize the opportunity to patiently explain such knowledge that children naturally crave. The proportional question that Emperor Ming answered was merely his father testing his intellectual agility. His statement that the sun is far away was a theoretical concept, while his statement that the sun is near was a poetic expression. He did not fundamentally understand these concepts but was able to unknowingly reconcile them to justify his answers. That is why he can be called a "genius!"

France Trains Young Aviators 170

— Ying Dai

The French government, recognizing the extremely dangerous and precarious times and the potential for a second European war, has determined that air power will be a primary force in any future conflict. Therefore, it has begun training young aviators. All children in schools, from ages nine to twenty-one, will undergo aviation training. The details of this plan have been finalized by the Minister of Aviation. France is initiating this aviation training for young students because its current pool of aviation personnel is insufficient to meet the demands of a potential world war. Additional young talent must be cultivated to fill the gaps. The training program will proceed in three stages.

First stage: Children ages nine to fourteen will receive introductory aviation knowledge.

Second stage: Children ages fourteen to seventeen will receive instruction in aviation science.

Third stage: Individuals ages eighteen to twenty-one will engage in practical flight training.

The Minister of Aviation of France has expressed that this training will greatly benefit both civilian and military aviation in France. It is also considered highly suitable for French youth. The Aviation Ministry will also establish a dedicated department to oversee this aviation training program. This training approach is cost-effective, but it will soon produce a large number of aviators, ensuring that all regions of France have aviation talent. Once training begins, periodic evaluations will be conducted. In short, French schools will soon implement aviation training, producing a vast number of young aviators.

Fish in a Cauldron 171

— Chen Tiewu

Little fish, swimming in a cauldron,

Swimming to and fro, unaware of sorrow;

Happily relying on the iron walls for protection,

Unworried when enemies arrive.

Fish in a cauldron, growing anxious,

The heat around its body gradually rising;

Suddenly hearing a "hissing" sound from the bottom of the cauldron,

Hoping for a breeze to dispel the warmth.

Joy and anxiety side by side.

Fish in a cauldron, finally awakened,

Self-assessing, no longer anxious,

Leaping over the dragon gate, ten thousand feet high;

Drawing itself out with a jump,

The lid of the pot firmly closed,

Flailing around a couple of times,

Its life expires in a final gasp.

Children:

Think about it, take a look around,

Our environment,

Our surroundings,

Are they strangely similar to the fish in a cauldron?

Our property,

Our lives,

Are they as precarious as the fish in a cauldron?

A Meaningless War 172

— Lan Shan

Once upon a time, the emperor of one country sent an official document to another country, which read: "Send me a blue pig with a black tail; otherwise--" The emperor of the other country replied with his own official document, "I don't have such a pig; if I did--"

The emperors of both countries were angered and declared war on each other. They gathered large armies and fought dozens of bloody battles. Many brave soldiers died, and many women and children were left without food or clothing, and many froze or starved to death.

Later, the emperors of both countries realized that their military forces were evenly matched, that neither could defeat the other, and that continuing the fight was futile. They both felt it necessary to negotiate a truce. But the first problem to be solved was to clearly explain the meaning of the official documents, because the emperor of Country A was not satisfied with the reply from Country B, and the emperor of Country B was not satisfied with the demands of Country A!

The emperor of Country B asked: "What did you mean by asking me to send you a blue pig with a black tail? Otherwise what?"

"Why?" said the emperor of Country A: "My meaning is very simple, I asked you to send me a blue pig with a black tail, otherwise any other color would do."

"Ah! Is that so?" said Emperor B, "I regret that I did not receive the full content of your official document!"

"But I must ask you," said Emperor A, "What was the meaning of your reply! 'I don't have such a pig; if I did--' What does that mean?"

"Oh," said Emperor B, "My official document is as simple as yours. I said I don't have such a pig; if I did, I could send it to you." "Alright! Alright!" said Emperor A, "We have fought a war in vain. If we had properly explained ourselves before the war, wouldn't all the losses and all the suffering have been avoided?"

Later, the emperors of both countries recorded this "black-tailed blue pig" war in their historical records, so that everyone would be vigilant at all times and avoid the recurrence of similarly pointless wars.

We Need to Wash Our Faces with Cold Water 173

— Jun Qi

Children! When we wake up in the morning, we must do a cleaning job of washing our faces and brushing our teeth, only then will we feel comfortable, this is due to the cleanliness of our skin. A person's skin has the function of regulating body temperature. Strong skin, able to withstand cold and heat, will become stronger and healthier day by day, and the spirit will be happy.

If we want to protect our bodies, we must first exercise our skin, and there are many ways to do this, with cold water washing being the best. However, there must be training, and it will take time to take effect; otherwise, not only will the body not become stronger, but serious diseases may also occur, which is something to pay close attention to. Therefore, before practicing the habit of cold water washing, the initial basic training is to wash the face with cold water: on the one hand, it is easy to train, and on the other hand, it will not cause disease.

Although cold water washing only involves two small parts, the hands and the face, because they are often in direct contact with the air, they should be exercised first, and then gradually to the whole body, then the good habit of cold water washing will be successful.

It is best to start washing your face with cold water in the summer. As the weather gets colder, we must still stick to our principles and persevere to the end. If we can survive the severe winter, after this habit is formed, not only will the skin become firm, but the body will also increase its health. This is very beneficial for children. I hope all children will strive to put it into practice!

The Earth and the Moon 174

— Jun Peng

On the night of the Mid-Autumn Festival, Fuyue, of course, was playing and jumping happily in his own yard, just like all the children, holding mooncakes in his hands, eating and laughing, shouting: "Moon! Moon! You look like a basin, like a bowl, come down and play!" Sitting on the chair, Fuyue's father pointed at the moon in the sky and said, "Fuyue! Do you know why the moon on Mid-Autumn Festival feels especially bright compared to any other full moon?" Fuyue was silent, and his father continued: "This is because the autumn night is clear and cool." Fuyue asked: "Where did the moon come from?" His father smiled and said: "The origin of the moon is really incredible. Millions and millions of years ago, the sun was rotating very fast in the sky, and because of the vibration of the rotation, a large piece separated and stood in the sky separately, following the sun and constantly rotating, and because of the rotation force being very far, the shape gradually became elliptical, this is the Earth". Later, the "Earth" was also like the sun. Tens of millions of years after the "Earth", because it was not a fireball, it gradually cooled down, but a small lump that looked like a wart grew on the surface of the "Earth" and gradually grew larger. Subjected to the vibration of rotation and the wave action of the sun, it suddenly left the "Earth" and rotated around the "Earth" constantly, also forming another one in the sky, this is the moon". Its volume is five thousand cubic miles, the diameter is three thousand four hundred and seventy-six, the distance from "Earth" is three hundred and eighty-four thousand and four hundred kilometers. To think of going to the moon for a walk, it would take more than a hundred days by plane and more than three hundred days by train, but it's only ideal, it is definitely impossible."

Fuyue's father, took a cigarette, and continued: "The light of the moon is reflected from the direct sunlight to the "Earth", as many as four billion lights. The brightest place we see is the volcano, and the darker places like mountains are the valleys and the sea. On the moon, half a month is daytime, and half a month is nighttime. The temperature during the day is above a hundred degrees, and at night it suddenly drops to hundreds of degrees below zero, so there is basically no atmosphere or water layer, and life goes without saying. The moon grows round from the first to the fifteenth of the month, and it decreases from the sixteenth to the thirtieth. Because of the different positions of the Sun, Earth, and Moon at times, sometimes the Moon is between the Sun and the Earth, just in a parallel line, which becomes a solar eclipse. The Earth is between the Sun and the Moon, also in a parallel line, which becomes a lunar eclipse."

The above conversation was heard when I went to Fuyue's house to play on the night of the Mid-Autumn Festival. I felt that it was very interesting and valuable, so I introduced it to everyone. I believe the children must be happy to hear it!

Children's Freehand Drawing - Country Factory 175

Pigeons 176

— Zhong Mei

Since Xiao Min asked Xiao Yong for a pair of pigeons during the summer vacation, he has been very careful to bathe them, feed them, clean the pigeon loft, etc. every day, so in the past two months, the pair of pigeons have grown very fat. Who wouldn't like the snow-white feathers lined with crimson eyes?

One day, when Xiao Min was working for them, his younger brother Ren'er asked him, "Brother Min, what kinds of pigeons are there in our poultry?" Xiao Min cleaned the pigeon loft while answering in a low voice, "Brother Ren, as far as I know, there are five kinds: first, eye-circle pigeons, second, pouter pigeons, third, carrier pigeons, fourth, wild pigeons, and fifth, peacock pigeons.

Brother Min, what are the uses of the pigeons you just mentioned? The uses of the pigeons I just mentioned are: 1. Eye-circle pigeons: around their eyes, like people wearing glasses, there is a layer of shiny things, so they are called eye-circle pigeons. In addition to being used for playing and raising, their eggs and meat can be eaten. 2. Pouter pigeons: Their chests are protruding, so they are called pouter pigeons. There is no difference between their use and that of eye-circle pigeons. 3. Carrier pigeons: Because of their strong memory and ability to fly back and forth from very far places, they are used to transmit messages in the army. 4. Wild pigeons: Their meat and eggs can be eaten, and other internal organs and feathers can be used as fertilizer. 5. Peacock pigeons: Their tail feathers are very long and can be opened and folded like a peacock, so they are called peacock pigeons. Their use is the same as that of eye-circle pigeons.

Brother Min, what are the differences between pigeons and chickens?

The differences between pigeons and chickens, in short, there are several points. Let's talk about pigeons first: 1. The beak is covered with soft skin except at the front end. 2. The hind limbs are very short and small. Male pigeons do not have spurs. 3. They are intelligent and easy to tame and do not like to fight. 4. It is not easy to tell the difference between male and female pigeons. 5. The wings are large and sharp, and they fly very fast. 6. They like to eat fruits and grains. As for chickens, 1. The entire beak is very hard and not covered with soft skin. 2. The hind limbs are strong, and the males have spurs. 3. They like to fight. 4. It is easy to tell the difference between male and female chickens. 5. The wings are short and cannot fly. 6. They like to eat insects, grains, and fruits.

Our Travel Journal 179

— Zhang Junxin of the Xin'an Travel Group

(My First Time in Shanghai)

'Shanghai is a very gorgeous and complex' city, there are many people, and foreign houses are everywhere'. I often hear people say this, but I, an old man from Jiangbei, have never been to this prosperous Shanghai. This time it's really an unexpected trip to Shanghai. How happy is this?

On the evening of the second day after arriving here, I found a few classmates to go out and see the sights. After walking a lot, I felt very strange; why is it not lively here? Just as I was wondering, one of my classmates said to me, "Hey! Don't you know? This is Jing'an Temple Road, so the first section should be quiet!", At this time, I thought to myself, that's true, there is even some foreign writing on the sign of Jing'an Temple Road in front, so it should be quiet here. Only then did I realize, no wonder there were only one man and one woman walking slowly, not even daring to speak loudly. In fact, there was also a car moving around. We walked forward again, and when we got to a place, a person suddenly came from the opposite side and shouted, 'Jiangbei pigs!' I asked my classmate again, "What does the word 'pigs' mean?" My classmate said, "It's cursing people." I said, "That's really strange, why does calling someone 'pigs' curse them?" This classmate said, "'Pigs' is what the locals here use to scold people from Jiangbei, but people from Jiangbei also scold people here, calling them 'chilao'!" Oh, I realized that "chilao" is what Shanghai people call "pigs" to scold people from Jiangbei. Not far away, I said, "Why are there so many foreigners here?" My classmate said: "Because this is a concession." At this time, I wondered again, why are there British concessions and French concessions? My classmate said to me again: "A concession is a Chinese place rented to England or rented to other countries, this is called a concession. So I asked, "How many concessions do we Chinese have in foreign countries?" My classmate said, "Do we Chinese still want to have concessions in foreign countries?" I asked again, "Why?" My classmate said, "It is because stronger countries always have concessions abroad." I thought to myself, why do stronger countries have concessions, and weaker nations have their land rented out to others? Isn't China a country whose land has been rented out to others? Isn't it also a weak nation?

Seven Sisters in the Mountains (3) 180

— Xin Qing

She checked the potatoes she had stored among the ferns outside again, thinking that if she brought them all into the house, the heat from the fireplace might spoil them. So, she only took a few, enough for them to eat one meal. Afterwards, she went to the cow and milked it, but the poor old creature was hungry, so it didn't give much milk, not enough to fully supply them. An Ge Ni knew she had to give it some hay. So, she called her two younger brothers to help her climb into the attic and start pulling down the hay, but they were just small children, and the work was too difficult. As night fell, the attic was pitch black, frightening the two younger brothers. Little An Ge Ni had to do it herself, pulling down a lot of hay, feeding the old cow until it was full, and bedding it down properly. Soon it was dinnertime, and the sisters gathered together, filling their stomachs. After the meal, An Ge Ni, just like the night before, undressed her twin little sisters, put them to bed, and sang them songs to soothe them to sleep. Seeing that they were all asleep, she and the rest of her siblings sat around the fireplace, waiting for their parents to return, listening intently for the sound of their loved ones outside the door, hour after hour. Sometimes, it seemed like they heard footsteps in the wind, and they would all hold their breath, waiting intently. After a while, the wind would pass, and everything would be as silent as death again. The snow was falling heavily again that night. An Ge Ni was careful to keep the doors and windows from being blocked by snow, and she was also careful about the fire in the fireplace, lest it be extinguished by the snow blowing down the chimney. She kept watch until midnight again, but still, she didn't see her father and mother return, nor did anyone else come to help them. She had no other choice but to go to bed. When she woke up, she saw that the snow was falling even heavier, dashing her last hope. Her dear and lively mother, and her strong and courageous father, were both good climbers. If they hadn't encountered any accidents, they would have returned long ago, after these two days. Poor little An Ge Ni barely made it to the third day, caring for her siblings as usual, everyone constantly praying, hoping that their parents would return home safe and sound.

On the morning of the fourth day, the snow had stopped, and the wind had changed direction. Much of the snow on the ground had been blown away. An Ge Ni immediately perked up. She and her sisters went out together, following a low stone wall, heading towards Grasmere. She avoided the danger of crossing the creek bridge and took a detour instead. They walked for a while and reached the mountain ridge. An Ge Ni quickly sent her siblings back and bravely continued forward alone, trudging through the vast snowy hillside, only wanting to find her parents, forgetting all the dangers, finally arriving at the door of the house closest to Grasmere.

An Ge Ni knocked on the door, and the people inside opened the door and welcomed her, but when she asked about her father and mother, their smiles immediately turned into worried expressions. Within half an hour, the news of the disappearance of the George Green couple had spread throughout the valley, and sixty strong men gathered in Gouke Town and set out together to search for them. According to the last people who saw them, after the auction that day, several friends had advised them not to walk the dangerous mountain road at night, but after they parted ways, their whereabouts were unknown. Some residents of Lantai said that they seemed to have heard shouts in the middle of the night, but they thought it was just the wind blowing, so they didn't pay attention to it.
